Post-War Inspection Record of the Longhai Railway 77

The Process of Recapturing Luoyang

The Current Status of Transportation on All Routes

Xuzhou Correspondence: After inspecting Zhengzhou for two days, the Xuzhou reporters planned to go to Luoyang, but were prevented by rain. However, they learned about the recent situation in western Luoyang in Zhengzhou, and continued to inspect the trenches in Zhengzhou. They left Zhengzhou at noon on the 18th and returned to Xuzhou. The sequel is as follows:

Luoyang Situation: Luoyang is 240 li west of Zhengzhou. Feng's army has a garrison commander stationed in Luoyang. Yang Hucheng's troops occupied Luoyang Station on the 10th. Garrison Commander Zhao Shouyu still guarded the city and closed the city for several days. Yang's troops and Xu Yuanquan's troops jointly surrounded it. Yang's forward troops had already passed through Luoyang and advanced westward. The Zhengzhou-west ticket train reached Luoyang East Station directly on the 14th. Zhao Shouyu's troops in the city, hearing the sound of the train whistle at the station, fired at the station. Finally, with no way to retreat, they negotiated surrender. The city gate was opened on the 16th. Xu Yuanquan is handling the aftermath in Luoyang, and will disarm and reorganize Zhao's troops. Yang Hucheng himself is also stationed at Luoyang Station, commanding his troops to advance westward. As of when the reporter left Zhengzhou, the ticket train could already reach Jinguyuan, the west station of Luoyang, but most of them were damaged factory cars. In addition, Luoyang City has just been captured, the disarmament has not been completed, and peace has not yet been fully achieved.

Military News from Western Luoyang: Feng's troops, including Song Zheyuan and Ge Yunlong's troops, retreated from western Luoyang. There was no resistance along the way, so there were no fierce battles. Song's troops initially went west along the railway line, and Yang Hucheng's troops pursued from behind. On the 17th, military news from western Luoyang was obtained, and Song's troops crossed the Yellow River north after passing through Shanzhou, heading towards Fenglingdu. Therefore, since the 17th, the telephone line on the Longhai Road has been connected to Tongguan. Yang Hucheng's pursuit troops, considering Tongguan's importance and the fact that Song's troops had already crossed the river, sent teams to defend the south bank of the Yellow River on the one hand, and continued to advance rapidly towards Tongguan on the other. Military news on the 18th stated that the forward troops had passed Hangu and reached Lingbao, and would arrive in Tongguan within a day. Military transport vehicles can already travel westward across Shanzhou. The Transportation Command has appointed Zhang Jiechao as the director of the Luoyang Office and Xu Lanting as the director of the Shanzhou Office. Zhang went west to Luoyang on the 15th, and Xu went west to Tongguan on the 18th, and established offices separately to handle military transportation at the front. As of the 18th, there were no Feng's troops east of Tongguan.

Zheng Suburb Battle Trenches: Before leaving Zhengzhou on the 18th, the reporter went to inspect the gathering point battle trenches of Feng's army three li east of Zheng Station. These trenches were built by Feng's army one month before retreating from Zhengzhou. Initially, Feng's army did not build defensive fortifications in Zhengzhou. After the successive defeats on the Longping lines at the front, they temporarily dug them to specifically protect Zhengzhou City Station. This type of battle trench is built in a special way, all around the village. A circular ditch is dug around the village, with a depth and width of about four to five feet. Behind the ditch is a small bunker, about three feet above the ground. On top of the bunker, there are concealing earth blocks, arranged on the bunker like sawtooths. The houses and trees in the village are used as natural concealment. Each village has the same effort. Between the village and the ditch, there are oblique and winding traffic trenches to connect them, which can be used for people to walk. Because the ditches are clustered around the village as densely as stars, the soldiers call them gathering point ditches. The construction of these ditches employed 10,000 civilians and took about two weeks.

Transportation Overview: The four roads of Zhengbu are open, and the Pinghan southbound ticket train is unobstructed. The northbound ticket train can already reach Rongze, and military vehicles can directly reach the south bank of the Yellow River. There is a small damage to the Yellow River Railway Bridge. The damage is at the southern end and has been repaired. Along the Longhai Road, willow trees are seen replacing sleepers along the way. The train travels very slowly, and the ticket trains are extremely crowded. The reporters left Zhengzhou at 3:30 pm on the 18th and arrived in Xuzhou at 12:00 pm on the 19th. The train cars were dark at night. They borrowed a horse lamp from the train guard to guard their luggage. Along the way, there was wind and rain, and the cold wind penetrated the empty windows without boards, making people want to stay silent. The rainfall along the way was sufficient. The drought in the sandy land of Henan Province was alleviated by this rain, which should benefit agriculture a lot. (19th)

Shandong Provincial Government Prepares to Redeem the Jiaoji Railway 78

Jinan Correspondence: Li Dufang, a standing committee member of the Economic and Financial Reorganization Committee of the Shandong Provincial Government, proposed to the Provincial Government to establish a Preparatory Committee for Redeeming the Jiaoji Railway to prepare for the redemption of the Jiaoji Railway. This proposal was passed by the standing committee of the committee today (22nd). It is heard that Han Fuqu, chairman of the provincial government, also strongly agrees with this matter. This case will be submitted for discussion at the provincial government standing committee this Friday (24th). The original case is recorded as follows: "For the proposal to prepare for the redemption of the Jiaoji Railway to develop Shandong's economy and finance, it is found that the Jiaoji Railway was decided by the Beijing government to be returned to China by the Japanese. Later, after negotiations between the Shandong Case Aftermath Committee and the Japanese envoy, it was valued at 40 million Japanese yen, and after receiving it, interest was paid for seven years, and the principal was repaid in eight years, to be redeemed in fifteen years. Counting from February 1, 1923, when it was formally received, the interest payment period expired on February 1 of this year, and the method of redemption should have been planned long ago. However, since the reception, wars have been frequent, and the political situation has changed repeatedly, and there has been no time to discuss redemption. In addition, at that time, the road had a board of directors that seized power and held it, abused private individuals, and shared the benefits. It is estimated that the annual income of the road over the years was more than 12 million yuan, of which more than 9 million yuan was used for interest on debt notes, salaries of employees, and regular bureau expenses, and more than 2 million yuan was used for purchasing materials. The annual surplus was only several hundred thousand yuan. The huge waste was unprecedented in the country. The board of directors was not happy to discuss redemption, and the central government and the Shandong government had no time to discuss redemption, allowing such a large property to be held by foreigners, which is very regrettable. It is found that the Jiaoji Railway line is more than 900 li long, running across the east and west, all in Shandong Province. It connects Qingdao, the tail of Asia, in the east, and Jinan, the capital of the province, in the west. It borrows Jinpu to the south and has the south goods of Longhai. It connects Cangshi to the north and gathers the transportation of Yan and Jin, all of which are exported to Qingdao through this road. It is truly the general hub of the economy and finance of Qi and Lu, and the lifeline of 37 million people. Moreover, when the road rights are in the hands of foreigners, they hold the interests of Shandong and control the fate of China. For example, the troops entered in May 3rd, causing strange changes at home and abroad, secretly assisting warlords, resulting in the remnants of Jiaodong, and privately transporting military fire and extensively selling drugs, manipulating bandits, and ravaging the interior. The economy of the people of the province is being destroyed and exploited day by day. How can it not be the case that the road rights are in the hands of foreigners? If we do not quickly redeem them, the people of Lu will never have peace, and the economy and finance of this province will not be able to develop. In the past, at the beginning of the reception of Jiaozhou, some people proposed that this road should be owned by the people, and the government also clearly ordered Gu Zhongxiu to be the supervisor of road redemption. Internal and external agencies and staff also deducted salaries as road redemption funds. However, it ended up failing. The only achievement was that the Jiaoji Road spent several more yuan to pay the salary of the supervisor, and the salary deducted by the staff also flowed to the reimbursement of the agency. As for the past governors and warlords of the province, they only cared about abusing the people to their heart's content. The previous provincial government could have done something at the time of the revolutionary unification, but it did not have time for this, nor could it mention this. Now, fortunately, our chairman is ordered to govern Lu, and he is greatly refreshing, consolidating the military and economy, working hard to govern, and looking forward to starting anew with the people of Lu. It is also the day of success in the anti-rebellion, and the Jiaoji Road should be redeemed. This is truly the only good fortune for Shandong, and it is also the only important task for our chairman to save Lu and save the people. If our chairman resolutely decides to prepare the foundation for road redemption, gradually formulate funds, lead the people, redeem it as scheduled, and do not hesitate to restore national sovereignty once, the people of Lu will be blessed for generations, and it will also be the glory of the whole country and the immortal great achievement that will shock the world. However, this matter is of great importance, and the investigation should be detailed, the consideration should be meticulous, and the planning should be careful. It cannot be hastily or recklessly planned, nor can it be fully explained in a few words. To summarize it, the main points can be roughly stated, such as determining whether the road rights are owned by the province or the country, abolishing the board of directors of the road, reorganizing the road administration income, formulating road redemption funds, and organizing a fund management committee. There are many items, which cannot be enumerated. At the beginning of the launch, the most important thing is to submit a request to the provincial government by this committee, submit it for discussion, and establish a road redemption preparatory committee. However, at the beginning of the preparation, do not expand the matter. It seems that it can be attached to this committee, the expenses can be slightly increased, and the staff does not need to be added. First, the members of this committee will be the members of the road redemption preparation. Those who are good at road administration or familiar with the Jiaoji Road situation, which are necessary for the preparation, will be rehired. After the preparation is slightly rudimentary and gradually successful, submit a case to the central government and set up another agency to implement the road redemption. It is not too late. This is a humble opinion of a committee member to initiate the redemption of the road in order to establish the fundamental outline of Shandong's economy and finance. Is it appropriate? I beg for public decision. Proposer: Standing Committee Member Li Dufang."

Guangdong Province Resumes Cashing Central Bank Notes 79

First Cash the Ten-Yuan and Five-Yuan Notes Issued by Huang Longsheng

Announces Suspension of Accepting Uncashed Banknote Deposits and Paying Interest

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province's finances have recently improved as the local war has ended and several million yuan worth of financial treasury bonds have been sold over the past few months. The Central Bank's fund is becoming more and more abundant. Recently, the funds for recognized and sold bonds from various parties have been fully deposited in the Central Bank. The authorities also believe that the value of the uncashed five-yuan and ten-yuan notes on the market is increasing due to the treasury bond sales. Recently, it has risen to 94% or 95% of its face value, which is not much different from the full price. Therefore, at the regular provincial affairs meeting on the 17th, a talk was held (because Chen Mingshu, Lin Yunxi, Sun Xiwen, Deng Yanhua, etc. have gone north and the quorum is not met), and the proposal to restore uncashed banknotes was raised. After a long discussion, it was decided to first unconditionally cash the five-yuan and ten-yuan notes signed in English by Huang Longsheng (former president of the Central Bank) and Zhou Siming (former vice president). It was decided to implement it on the 20th of this month, and the rest will be cashed successively at the beginning of next month. After receiving the order, the Central Bank has actively prepared. It is found that there are only 3 million Central Bank notes circulating outside. The bank has prepared considerable cash, and it will be easy to cope with it. As for the Beihai and Meilu branches in the South Road, the head office also telegraphed them to resume business immediately. Huang Shiguang, the head of the Beihai branch, and his staff have transported the cash of the branch by the warship Hairui. As for Huang Yufang, the head of the Meilu branch, he escorted the cash to Meilu on the 17th. Once he arrives, he can resume business. As the uncashed banknotes on the market have been scheduled to be cashed, the Central Bank announced on the 16th that it would stop accepting uncashed banknote deposits and pay interest to end the previous absorption method. The bank has issued the following notice: "It is found that this bank has submitted a request to the Guangdong Provincial Government for approval to accept uncashed banknotes, and to fix the term and pay interest on deposits. The starting period is from August 1st of this year to the end of October. It has been notified to the public. Now it is found that the period is about to expire, and the market needs more and more various banknotes of this bank. There are very few merchants and people who come to the bank to deposit. This deposit should be stopped from the 16th of this month, and the interest on the demand deposit that has not been withdrawn will also be stopped from this day to end it. As for the time deposit, interest will still be calculated until the full three months. In addition to reporting, this is a special notice." (October 18th)

Guangzhou Continued News: The Central Bank opened to cash five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes yesterday (20th). First, the acting president Fan Qiwu was ordered by the provincial government to open the five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes with English signatures of Huang Longsheng and Zhou Siming on the 20th. Since the 19th was a Sunday holiday, he ordered the staff on the 18th to prepare all the matters for the opening of the exchange to avoid temporary troubles. At the same time, the business section was ordered to allocate the prepared funds to the head office, the Xidi branch, and the Yonghan exchange office to prepare for citizens to come to cash. At 9:00 am yesterday morning, the Central Head Office, the Xidi Branch, and the Yonghan Office started cashing at the same time. At about 8:00, the president and vice president Fan Qiwu and Shen Zaihe arrived at the head office by car to direct the handling of everything. It was found that the cashing method on that day was in accordance with the provincial government's order. Only the five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes with English signatures of Huang Longsheng and Zhou Siming were cashed. The rest of the five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes with Chinese signatures were not exchanged. Therefore, those who did not understand the procedure and held the above-mentioned Chinese banknotes to cash were politely explained by the staff, and they were asked to wait for the order to open the exchange before bringing them to cash again. On that day, the cashing order was extremely small due to the few people who came to cash, and there were special police officers protecting and maintaining it in front of the door, so there was no disorder. As for the Xidi Branch and the Yonghan Exchange, after receiving the funds allocated by the head office, they also started cashing five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes at the same time. The number of people who came to cash was even smaller. According to statistics, the head office cashed only more than 10,000 yuan in the morning, and only about 30,000 yuan in the afternoon. The total amount cashed by the Xidi Branch and the Yonghan Exchange was about 50,000 yuan for the whole day. According to the investigation of the Central Bank, the total amount of this banknote circulating on the market is about 3 million yuan, of which more than 1 million yuan are five-yuan notes and more than 1 million yuan are ten-yuan notes. The total fund owned by Zhonghe is more than 10 million yuan. In addition to the cashing reserve for one-yuan and one-hundred-yuan banknotes accounting for more than 6 million yuan, the rest is enough to cope with the cashing of five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes with English signatures and there is a surplus. The general merchants and people therefore have this banknote, which is fully circulated on the market, and the Central Bank has sufficient funds and stable credit, so most of them do not go to cash it to save procedures. Most of those who come to cash are partners of various silver houses, all of whom are cashing small amounts of two or three hundred yuan. (21st)

A Terrible Fire in Wuzhou 80

A fire broke out on a raft in the Fuyi River in Wuzhou on the afternoon of the 17th, killing and injuring dozens of men and women, and causing property losses of more than 300,000 yuan. At about 3:30 pm, near the Jinling Restaurant staircase, a stove was set up close to the wooden walls of the house. The partners placed too much firewood, causing the wooden walls to catch fire. The fire spread quickly. The facade and staircase of the Jinling Restaurant were first ignited, and then spread to the large and small boats parked near the raft. The fire became more intense and spread to the Lingnan Restaurant, Xinfa, Fu'anfa, Tianhefa, Anxingfa, etc. All nearby flower boats were burned. The bamboo and wooden houses on the riverbank from the iron pillar pier to the Shixiang mouth were also affected. The windows and doors of the Guangtaiyu and Liang stores on Jiufang Road were also ignited, but fortunately, the rescue was effective and it did not spread. Otherwise, the stores along Jiufang Road would have been unimaginable. When the fire spread, the nearby rafts could not escape, and the wooden rafts and boats that were farther away drove out of the river to avoid the fire. Two rafts, Yongcheng and others, hired fire boats and towed them to the river surface of the iron pillar pier. The rest of the large and small boats also rushed to open, or drove to the Huoshan River to park. The river surface from the Fuyi River mouth to Helongzhou was full of large and small boats and wooden rafts, flowing down with the water, rushing to escape. The situation was extremely panicked. The prostitutes Nantongmei and the boat girls of the raft rushed ashore, in a state of disarray. The fire alarm tower of the fire brigade in Dongmen immediately rang the bell to warn, and all water carts and water dragons arrived to put out the fire. The fire engines of the fire brigade of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the two fire boats of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce drove to the center of the Fuyi River, spraying water towards the fire on the rafts. The water carts of the Chengxiang Fire Service Branch, the Xinglongfang water carts, and the Wutongfang water carts were stationed at Wuxian Pier, Tiezhuzi Pier, and Shixiang Mouth to put out the fire. At 4:50, the fire gradually slowed down, and the stores along Jiufang Road were able to be preserved. At 5:30, the fire was completely extinguished. The fire brigade of the Municipal Public Security Bureau still watered the remaining embers one by one to avoid re-ignition. The Sixth Third Division Supplementary Regiment of the Headquarters, the Security Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and the police stations in various districts all sent teams to suppress the situation at Jiufang Road, Tiezhuzi Pier, Wuxian Pier, and Shixiang Mouth. The headquarters also sent Browning pistol teams and military police to the west gate to strictly guard against accidents. The Water Police Department also used ships to carry armed police to patrol the river. Therefore, the order at that time was extremely peaceful. The teams did not return to their units until 6:00. Although the deaths and injuries caused by this fire could not be accurately investigated for a while, they were generally more than 30 or 40 people. Most of them were killed by drowning. Seven wooden rafts and dozens of flower boats and other large and small boats were burned. All the flower wine wooden rafts and boats were burned. A total of more than 40 bamboo and wooden houses on the riverbank were burned. The total loss was no less than 300,000 yuan, which is a rare disaster in recent years.

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 81

The Jiangdu Fugitive Case Transferred to Zhenjiang Local Court for Review: Chen Quan, the former director of the Jiangdu County Court Detention Center, was dismissed by the High Court for escaping 57 prisoners during the Mid-Autumn Festival and sent to the county court for legal proceedings. Yesterday (24th), Chief Justice Lin of the High Court instructed Chen Ruizhen, the president of the county court, to transfer Chen Quan and the head of the detention center to the Zhenjiang Local Court Prosecutor's Office for investigation according to law.

Wuxi 82

Negotiations After the Closure of the Silk Weaving Factory: The Wuxi Silk Weaving Factory in Mianhua Lane outside the Ximen Gate of this county was opened by eight people including Rong Jianming and Li Yuren with a total share of 8,200 yuan, and a distribution office was set up at the Shuyuan Lane entrance in the city. However, due to the poor quality of the factory's products and sluggish sales, all the above-mentioned shares were completely lost. Shareholder Li Yuren became ill due to anxiety and passed away. Subsequently, after a meeting of shareholders, a solution was maintained. It was decided that Li's wife, Ms. Yang, would borrow 1,000 yuan from a certain money house, and certain shareholders would guarantee 4,000 yuan, so that the goods could continue to be shipped. Recently, the factory was unable to turn around and announced its closure. Ms. Li Yang's垫欵, with 20 pieces of woven silk as 800 yuan, and 200 yuan of capital, and 120 yuan of interest, was guaranteed by the manager Rong Jianming, and returned in full after the distribution office was sold. Yesterday, the lady learned that the distribution office had been sold and received 490 yuan. She immediately demanded payment from Rong Jianming, but Rong shirked in every possible way and did not fulfill the previous agreement. He was immediately arrested by the first branch of the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Inspector Qin opened a preliminary trial, and the testimonies of both parties were different. He ordered the prisoner to be escorted to the General Administration for transfer to the county government for review. Another Dispute Arises in Ruifeng Silk Factory: The three silk factories of Xiyi Defeng, Ruichang, and Qianfeng have recently experienced strikes one after another. Fortunately, the mediation was appropriate, and nothing happened. However, a dispute suddenly broke out in Ruifeng Silk Factory under Yinglong Bridge outside the West Gate. The reason was that the factory's assistant managers Wang Huitang and Wang Jiqing suddenly announced the suspension of work yesterday, intending to rely on two days of bonus work (according to the labor-capital agreement, two days of bonus work is relied on for every ten days of work). They claimed that raw materials would not be received until November 2nd. The workers were extremely angry when they heard the news. After the county party rectification committee and the people's training committee received the news, they sent Lu Zhenwen to mediate. Lu 君 consulted with the female workers' heads and Wang Huitang and Wang Jiqing, and they agreed to start the car on the 28th of this month. If it is not implemented, the bonus work must also be paid. The female workers thought that verbal agreement was not enough, and asked the labor and capital to sign an agreement to keep the letter. However, Tu Huitang and others insisted on not agreeing. The female workers were very angry and started yelling. After Lu Zhenwen persuaded them again and again, Wang Huitang sent the chief Che Shiqing to sign the agreement as a representative first. The female workers were satisfied and dispersed.

Suspected Thieves Escorted to the County for Investigation: The detective team of the Public Security Bureau of Xiyi County captured eight suspected thieves, including Gu Yanjiang, outside the West Gate the day before yesterday. It is reported that yesterday afternoon, the Public Security Bureau prepared documents to escort them to the county together. After being tried by trial officer Yu in court, except for Gu Yanjiang, who stuttered in his confession and was slightly suspicious, he ordered the temporary detention of the others. The other seven people, including Zhao Rongxi and Ma Da, were all innocent, and the reporter Zhao Xingpei could not point out the facts of the case, or there was a suspicion of framing with a grudge, so he ordered them to be released on bail together and await summons for verification and investigation.

Zhenjiang 83

Petition to Increase Prison Capacity: The original prisoner quota for Zhenjiang County Prison was 130, but there are currently over 300 male and female convicts who have been sentenced. In addition, the Jiangsu Provincial Security Department has sent over 120 prisoners for detention. There are only 20 large and small prison cells, housing over 400 prisoners, which is extremely crowded and difficult to accommodate more. Meanwhile, the number of convicts sentenced by the local court for execution and prisoners sent by the Security Department for detention continues to increase. It is rumored that the County Government plans to build additional prison cells in the open space in front of the prison and has petitioned the High Court and the Security Department to allocate funds for construction.

Jiangsu Provincial Government Sets Deadline for Completion of Zhongzheng Road: Construction on Zhongzheng Road in the Jiangsu Provincial capital began half a year ago. Recently, it has been reported that the Provincial Government is concerned about the slow progress, which is hindering traffic, and has ordered the Provincial Capital Construction Engineering Office to complete the project by November without further delay. It is reported that Tang Ying, the director of the Provincial Capital Construction Engineering Office, has instructed his subordinates to step up supervision of the work to ensure its completion on schedule. Furthermore, the section of road from the end of the main road to the New West Gate has many curves due to the presence of houses. This has resulted in frequent collisions and injuries to pedestrians. In view of this, the Construction Engineering Office is currently planning to demolish the houses in the curved sections and convert the road into a straight one. The houses on both sides of the narrow sections have also been marked for demolition to facilitate traffic.

Arrest of Muyang Counter-Revolutionary Fugitive in Xian: Wang Fuzhi, a fugitive counter-revolutionary from Muyang, was previously prosecuted by the County Party Committee for supporting the corrupt former County Magistrate Dong Shenghan in leading a crowd to destroy the Third Branch of the Xiguan District. He was sentenced to imprisonment by the County Government. Fearing the law, Wang fled and secretly came to Zhenjiang, staying at Jiang Yulong Inn by the river. He secretly associated with Song Huiting, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce who had previously aided the rebels in the province by extorting donations, with the intention of engaging in other activities. Recently, the Public Security Bureau detected this and arrested him yesterday afternoon at 6:00 PM. He is currently detained in the bureau, and it is said that he will be escorted back to Muyang for prosecution as soon as the request for his extradition arrives.

Agricultural Department Explains Use of Agricultural Bank Funds: The Jiangsu Province farmers’ bank funds collected from each county were originally converted from the two-cent per mu donation during the Sun Chuanfang era. In the northern Jiangsu counties, because the rebel army was in the area, funds were urgently needed, and most of the collection was carried out in the 15th and 16th years of the Republic. Moreover, because separate receipts were printed, the collection was not included in the Ding Pu levy, resulting in lower receipts than the Ding Pu levy and a significant shortfall. People misunderstood that this fund would also be canceled because taxes before the 15th year had been exempted, making collection difficult. Yesterday, the Agricultural Department issued a sincere notice to the 35 northern Jiangsu counties, stating that the Farmers’ Bank was established to support the development of the rural economy. Although the current funds collected were converted from the previous mu donation, their use is now implemented for agriculture, which is very different from the previous allocation for military needs. It urged everyone to actively contribute and not misunderstand.

Nantong 84

Aftermath of Bandit Suppression in Tonghai Counties: The bandit disturbances in Nantong and Haimen counties have been quelled, and land and water transportation are gradually recovering. Meanwhile, efforts are being made to expedite the organization of security corps and to rehabilitate refugees. County Magistrates Zhang Dong and Wu Yaochun have gone to the bandit areas to provide guidance on these efforts. The Department of Education has ordered the County Government to close the Shatianyian case. The Department of Education stated that the dispute between the Bureau of Education's undertaking of the Yicheng Shatianyian and the Jishengan has been resolved by the Provincial Government. Recently, the Bureau of Education has repeatedly reported losses, and therefore the County Government is ordered to quickly recover the sixth and seventh dike fields and to arrest the sand ruffians Zhang Hongxiang, Xu Daochun, and Wu Xingchi to facilitate the closure of the case.

Liquidation Measures for Huaihai Bank: The Huaihai Bank has been stranded in recent years due to the influence of the textile, salt reclamation, and securities industries. Recently, the shareholders' meeting decided to liquidate assets, make every effort to recover cash, and then set a new direction. Currently, for loans to yarn factories, it can join the debt group to recover them in sequence. Salt reclamation debt tickets and loans for various reclamation lands are to be used to demarcate land for interest collection or sold for realization.

Second Robbery of Fanshao Small Steamer: Yongxin Company's Fanshao small steamer was previously robbed at Qiushuge. Banditry Case Also Noted: At Hengqian Village in the county, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived the day before yesterday, each carrying guns and weapons. Tragic Bandit Situation in Yuanjiaji: After Yuanjiaji in the Third District of Huaiyin was disturbed by bandits on the 18th at dawn, Yuan Fanxian, the town leader of the village, came to the city to request the County Government to conduct an on-site investigation. According to him, the bandits destroyed fifteen tiled houses and over three thousand thatched houses in the village. A total of over two hundred households were affected by the disaster, which has become a scene of scorched earth. Currently, the disaster-stricken people are sleeping in the open air and exposed to the elements, and the sounds of crying fill the fields. People have no home to return to, and they are requesting that various charitable organizations provide relief on their behalf.

Team Leader Zhu Arrested: Zhu Jie, the former police team leader of Huaiyin, was dismissed from his post in spring by provincial order, and Yu Meisheng was appointed as the Huaiyin team leader. At the same time, he dispatched a large number of mounted police to pursue the ship. Suicide by Drowning After Debt Collection Arrest: Xu Wenkui, a resident of Dijia Village, Dongguan Street, was owed 60 yuan and a Hangzhou silk long gown by Zhang Liben, who runs the Xinxin Bathhouse. He demanded repayment but was refused. He sought mediation and moved furniture from Zhang's concubine's residence as collateral. Zhang sued, and the First Branch arrested Xu for three days, ordering him to return the original items and refusing to handle the debt dispute or allow him to go to court. Xu was extremely resentful and left a suicide note before drowning himself. Yesterday (the 22nd), his wife crossed the river to search for the body but was unable to find it, which is truly tragic.

Son-in-Law Suspected of Stabbing Mother-in-Law: Zhao Chen, a resident of Xujing Town in the county, has a daughter who is married to Li Qian. The night before last, Qian returned home from outside and caught a glimpse of his wife chatting intimately with his younger brother, Chen. Enraged, Qian smashed the objects, creating a commotion. Zhao Chen heard the noise and rushed over to scold Qian. Qian became even more enraged and grabbed a kitchen knife from the kitchen, stabbing Zhao six times. Murder of Husband Case: The ringleader dies in prison. Jiangbei resident Zong Er was hired to work at the home of Shi Tonghai in Jiaochang Village, Xixiang. Unexpectedly, his wife, Pan, became secretly acquainted with Zong Er. The two planned to spend their lives together and bribed Wang Sanzi and others to help them murder her husband. After the incident was exposed, the County Government sent police to arrest all the perpetrators. They confessed without hesitation. The murderous woman, Shi Pan, became depressed after the confession and fell ill. She died in prison on the 23rd of this month. The Russian men insisted on exchanging the banknote, but Lu refused, leading to an unsuccessful transaction and an unpleasant departure. In the afternoon, Lu was on his way to Nanmen when he encountered the Russian men, who suddenly slapped him twice. Judge Zhang immediately held a court hearing. The Russian men, speaking Chinese, claimed their name was Amitov, they were opera performers, and they had come to Jiading to investigate whether they could operate their business here. Preparing to Organize Audit Office: The Zhejiang Provincial Government believes that many of its affiliated agencies, such as the Financial Review Committee, the Provincial Design Committee, the Provincial Final Accounts Committee, the Regulations Review Committee, and the Economic Committee, have similar functions and could be merged. Ningbo 94

Tenant Forced to Hang Himself: Yao Ruihe, the owner of Yaoyuantai Tinware Store on Yushi Tianning Temple Main Street, has been running his tinware store for over fifty years. The store is rented from Lin Yougen, with an annual rent of 40 yuan. Recently, a small vegetable market is being built near the Xiaojiaochang near the store. The landlord, Lin, thought he could make a profit and used this as an excuse to increase the rent fourfold, requiring a full year's rent of 160 yuan in advance. Yao Ruihe agreed to increase the rent by 60 yuan, but Lin still refused and forced him to leave the house. Yao Ruihe became depressed and hanged himself upstairs at around 1:00 PM the day before yesterday. Yao's son, Yunhe, believes that his father's death was caused by the landlord's forcing him to raise the rent. He is very unwilling and has reportedly filed a lawsuit with the court yesterday.

Two Robbery Cases: At the home of Chen Da Wen in the Ancestral Hall Village of Simen Township, Yuyao, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived the night before last, wielding firearms and flashlights. They broke down the door and looted. The bandits, seeing that there were not many boxes, cages, or valuables, and unable to satisfy their desires, kidnapped Chen Dawen's two-year-old grandson. Chen's wife, seeing her grandson being taken away, pleaded with the bandit leader. As a result, she paid the bandits 800 yuan, and the bandits left the child. Furthermore, the Fucheng Nunnery in Baishudi, more than ten li outside of Wusheng Gate in the north of Yuyao City, is located in a remote area with no neighbors. Only an elderly woman named Yu lives in the nunnery. The night before last, five or six bandits suddenly arrived, seized the elderly woman, and demanded silver. As a result, the elderly woman had no silver to give. The bandits then robbed her cotton quilt, clothes, and over ten yuan in cash before leaving.

Bengbu 95

Martyr Ma Xiangbin to Be Buried at Bengshan: Ma Xiangbin, also known as Wenbo, the commander of the Provisional Eleventh Army of the National Revolutionary Army, served the Party and the country for many years. Unfortunately, he died in battle in Haozhou two years ago. After the martyr was killed in Jinan, his coffin was transported back to his original residence in Suzhou. Later, the martyr's family surveyed and determined the location below Bengshan here as the cemetery and built a mausoleum. Construction has now begun. The martyr's bronze statue, commissioned by the famous Shanghai sculptor Li Jinfu, has now been completed. The statue is cast in bronze, eight feet high, and very lifelike. The casting cost seven thousand yuan.

Educational News

Important News

CU Undertakes Reform 98

School Affairs Meeting Discusses the Independence of Expenses for Each College

Sixty-Five Students Deny the Eighteen Demands

|School Affairs Meeting to Be Reorganized|

The School Affairs dispute at National Central University (CU) took a sharp turn yesterday (the 23rd). Secretary-General Zhang Zuoshi has resigned and left the school. Here is an account of yesterday's events.

(1) The School Affairs Meeting discussed the method of independent expenses for each college. The school convened its 21st School Affairs Meeting the day before yesterday and resolved to organize an independent expenses committee for each college. Here is an account of the meeting: Attendees: Xu Peikun, Zhang Naiyan, Cheng Zhenji (representing Xu Peikun), Zhao Lianfang, Xie Guansheng (representing Yu Nenmo), Wang Dong, Chen Maoxie (representing Lu Zhihong), Zhang Heng (representing Cheng Zongyu), Zou Bingwen (representing Sun Enqing), Qian Xiangbiao, Cai Bao, Huang Pu Huan, Hu Shanheng, Liu Mo; Yan Fuqing (representing Zhao Yunwen); Hong Fanwu (representing Jin Kai). Present: Zhang, Lu Miannan. Chairman: President Zhang. Recorder: Yang Minxiu. The meeting commenced as scheduled. The Chairman reported that the proposals passed by the Deans' meeting yesterday were submitted to this meeting for resolution and implementation. According to previous examples, each proposal was discussed item by item. (1) Proposal to amend the curriculum of each department: 1. In accordance with the established principles, the Curriculum Amendment Committee shall formulate detailed proposals. Resolution: Passed. 2. A committee should be organized to discuss detailed methods for amending the curriculum. The committee members shall be elected by the School Affairs Meeting. Resolution: Passed. President Zhang, Dean Huang, the deans of each college, and the professors' representatives from each college to the School Affairs Meeting were nominated as members of the Curriculum Amendment Committee (which will hold its first meeting at 3:00 PM today). (2) Proposal on whether the school's budget needs to be revised in the future: Resolution: After the curriculum is amended, the budget will be revised again in light of the Ministry of Education's expense standards for each college and the school's special circumstances. (3) Proposal on independent expenses for each college: Resolution: A committee will be organized to discuss detailed methods, which will be submitted to this meeting for approval. Hu Shanheng, Qian Xiangbiao, Cai Bao, Lu Shusen, and Dai Chongen were nominated as members of the Independent Expenses Discussion Committee for each college, to be convened by Hu Shanheng. (4) Proposal to formulate a training plan: Resolution: The Training Committee shall formulate a plan and submit it to the School Affairs Meeting for approval, and amend Article 2 of the committee's charter, changing the number of members to fifteen. Ai Wei, Zong Baihua, Xu Xiang, Xue Shaoqing, Tang Yangyu, Fang Guangqi, Cai Bao, Wang Dong, Huang Pu Huan, Lu Zhihong, Zhang Naiyan, Hu Shanheng, Yu Nenmo, Zhao Lianfang, and Liu Shu were nominated as members of the Training Committee, to be convened by Huang Pu Huan. (5) Proposal to actively promote physical education: Resolution: The Physical Education Committee shall formulate a plan and submit it to the School Affairs Meeting for approval, and amend Article 2 of the committee's charter, changing the number of members to seven. Lu Songen, Jin Zhaojun, Xu Xiang, a German (absent), Zhang Huilan, Hu Huanyong, and Zhang Naiyan were nominated as members of the Physical Education Committee. (6) Proposal from students from Hunan Province to be exempted from paying fees for this semester: Resolution: Before a decision is made, they will be allowed to defer payment for another month. The meeting adjourned at 12:30 PM.

(2) Students Deny Eighteen Demands: Yesterday, 65 students, including Ma Xiyuan, Cai Xu, and Huang Longwen, posted a notice stating that the eighteen demands for improving school affairs proposed by Ji Zicheng and over 600 others did not match the terms listed when they signed their names and involved attacks on individuals. They declared that they had not been informed of these matters beforehand, that they were clearly using their names to mislead the public, and that they could not take responsibility for them.

(3) School Affairs Meeting to Be Reorganized: Zhang Naiyan expressed great sympathy for the students' demands to reorganize the School Affairs Meeting with the principle of professors running the school and for the independent expenses of each college. Several days ago, he convened a group of professors to discuss the method of producing professor representatives and asked several specialists to draft a plan. It is said that it will be submitted for discussion at the next School Affairs Meeting so that the association can be formally reorganized.

Ministry of Education Orders the Promulgation of the Implementation Rules for the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline 99

The Ministry of Education will issue a notice to the education departments of each province and city to implement the implementation rules for the student self-government association organization outline approved by the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee.

Notice

Approved by the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee, document number 16601. The Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline was previously resolved and promulgated and has been instructed to comply with. To determine the organizational procedures of the Student Self-Government Association, the supervisory organs, and the relationship with the school to facilitate implementation, the Central Committee's 112th Standing Committee approved the Implementation Rules for the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline. In addition to the promulgation of the notification, a copy is attached for your reference and for the relevant agencies under your jurisdiction to be informed. Attached is a copy of the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline Implementation Rules for your reference and for the relevant agencies under your jurisdiction to be informed. It is hereby ordered that one copy of the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline Implementation Rules be copied and distributed.

Implementation Rules for the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline

Article 1: The local senior party department referred to in the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline refers to the county party department in the county and the city party department or special city party department in the city.

Article 2: The competent authority referred to in the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline is the county government in the county and the municipal government in the city.

Article 3: The organizational procedures of the Student Self-Government Association shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of Section 3 of the People's Organization Plan.

Article 4: After the initiators of the Student Self-Government Association receive the license certificate, they must establish a preparatory committee within four weeks, and the preparatory committee shall formulate a draft constitution for the Student Self-Government Association and submit it to the local senior party department for approval. When the preparatory committee is organizing, it must ask the school to send personnel to provide guidance.

Article 5: The preparatory committee shall register members, convene a meeting to pass the constitution, select staff, and establish a student self-government association within six weeks after the local senior party department approves the draft constitution.

Article 6: When the Student Self-Government Association has completed its organization, it must submit its constitution, staff resumes, and membership roster to the local senior party department for approval and then report to the school and the competent authority for the record.

Article 7: The membership roster of the Student Self-Government Association must include the following items: 1. Member number, 2. Name, 3. Native place, 4. Gender, 5. Age, 6. Grade, 7. Whether or not a member of the Kuomintang, 8. Address and mailing address. The staff resume of the Student Self-Government Association must include the above items and add a current position item.

Article 8: When each grade or college department elects representatives according to the proportion of members, the number of representatives and the proportion of people shall be determined by the Student Self-Government Association.

Article 9: When the Student Self-Government Association holds a membership meeting or a representative meeting, it must ask the local senior party department and the school to send personnel to provide guidance.

Article 10: If the Student Self-Government Association establishes a cooperative or a special committee, it must be resolved by the membership meeting, approved by the school, and reported to the local senior party department for the record.

Article 11: The Student Self-Government Association must request the school to send personnel to provide guidance on the progress of academic, sports, recreational, cooperative, and special committee work.

Article 12: If the resolutions of the Student Self-Government Association violate the provisions of Article 15 of the Student Self-Government Association's organization or exceed the scope of the Student Self-Government Association's duties, the school may revoke them.

Article 13: If the members of the Student Self-Government Association have any opinions on the improvement of school affairs, they may make suggestions to the school.

Article 14: The methods for the members of the Student Self-Government Association to practice and use the four rights of election, recall, initiation, and referendum shall be determined separately.

Article 15: These implementation rules shall be resolved and implemented by the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang.

Ministry of Education Requests the Executive Yuan to Issue an Order Prohibiting the Unauthorized Awarding of Honorary Degrees 100

Before the Promulgation of the Degree Awarding Law

The Ministry of Education recently presented a document to the Executive Yuan proposing that public and private universities should not be allowed to award honorary degrees without authorization before the Degree Awarding Law is enacted. The document stated that the establishment of degrees is for the purpose of honoring academics and encouraging future generations. The granting of degrees in European, American, and Japanese countries is extremely solemn, because titles cannot be given lightly. If they are abused slightly, they will damage their dignity. The Degree Awarding Law in our country is being carefully drafted by the Legislative Yuan. Before it is enacted and promulgated, it is proposed that public and private universities should not be allowed to award honorary degrees without authorization in order to emphasize the importance of titles and prevent abuse.

Economic Society's Hangzhou Branch Makes Efforts 104

In recent years, the Economic Society of China has been making rapid progress. In addition to the main society, branches have been established in major ports. The Hangzhou branch, since its establishment last year, has achieved considerable results. Its organization is quite simple, consisting of a president, vice-president, and secretary-cum-accountant, unlike the main society which has a board of directors. Both the president, Jin Runquan, and the vice-president, Jiang Zuomin, are very responsible and dedicated. The branch's expenses are raised independently, without relying on the main society. The branch's office has been temporarily borrowed from the Financial Personnel Training Institute, for which Vice-President Jiang Zuomin is responsible for the construction. The two Baoshan Western-style houses allocated by the provincial government earlier can only be moved into after the municipal government repairs the Baochu Pagoda. The members hold a monthly dinner, which is well attended. Members take turns hosting, and before the meal, a meeting is held to discuss matters or economic issues. All members are free to express their opinions.

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Institute in Wuxi, for the purpose of trialing urban mass education implementation methods this year, has specifically established an experimental Mass Education Center at the South Gate of Wuxi. Municipal Education Bureau Promotes Phonetic Symbols 106

In order to promote phonetic symbols, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has organized the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Phonetic Symbol Promotion Committee. The bureau has appointed all section chiefs, supervisors, and national language inspectors Xu Zeyi, Jiang Hongqi, Tang Shouqian, Zheng Tan, Ma Chonggan, Li Dachao, Yao Jibi, Wei Shinan, and Chen Yu, as well as experts Fang Xun’guang and Jiang Jingfu, as members of the committee. It has also formulated nine articles of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Phonetic Symbol Promotion Committee Organizational Rules, which have been submitted to the municipal government for approval and filing. The articles of the rules are excerpted below: 1. This bureau, in accordance with Article 9 of the Ministry of Education's Phonetic Symbol Promotion Committee Regulations, establishes the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Phonetic Symbol Promotion Committee (hereinafter referred to as this Committee) in order to promote the widespread implementation of phonetic symbols. 2. The number of members of this Committee shall be between nine and fifteen. 3. Members of this Committee are divided into ex-officio members and appointed members. I. Ex-officio members are the section chiefs, supervisors, and national language inspectors of this bureau, appointed by the bureau director. II. Appointed members are those who have a background in phonetic symbols and are interested in them, and may be selected and appointed as members by the bureau director. 4. This Committee shall have one chairman, who shall be appointed by the bureau director from among the members. 5. The affairs of this Committee are temporarily divided into the following sections: (I) Design Section: Planning and implementing measures for the implementation of phonetic symbols. (II) Publicity Section: Engaging in the publicity and lecturing of phonetic symbol writing and illustrations. (III) Guidance Section: Supervising and guiding the promotion of phonetic symbols in various districts. 6. The affairs of each section shall be undertaken by the respective members. 7. Regular meetings shall be held every two weeks, convened by the chairman. Extraordinary meetings may be convened when necessary. 8. Any matters not covered in these rules may be submitted to the bureau affairs meeting for amendment at any time. 9. These rules shall be promulgated and implemented after being approved by the bureau affairs meeting.

Wuben Girls' Middle School Celebrates 29th Anniversary 108

Shanghai Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School and its affiliated elementary school were founded by Wu Huaijiu in the 26th year of the Guangxu era of the Qing Dynasty, and have now been in existence for 29 years. Initially, it was a private school, then it was changed to a county school, and then in March of the 17th year of the Republic of China, it was changed to a municipal school of Shanghai. The school held a memorial meeting yesterday (the 24th). Xu Jinfu, representative of the Municipal Party Department, Guo Shihui, representative of the Mayor, Director Xu of the Education Bureau, and guests such as Ni Wenya, attended. At 9:00 AM, after the flag-raising ceremony, the memorial meeting was opened. After the ceremony was performed, Principal Wang Xiaoying reported on the brief history of the school and future new plans. Xu Yefu, representative of the Municipal Party Department, gave a speech, stating that your school is the oldest girls' school in Shanghai, and the significance of the anniversary is to celebrate the past and pray for the future. It is hoped that after 29 years, it will be more advanced than the 29th anniversary of the Wuben Girls' School (photo taken by this newspaper).

In the past nineteen years, there has been more progress, and in the future, it will be of great benefit to women's education in China. Guo Shihui, representative of the Mayor, gave a speech, stating that it is not easy for a school to have a history of 29 years. It is hoped that Principal Wang, all teachers and staff, and all students will continue to work hard so that the 30th anniversary next year will be even more successful. Director Xu of the Education Bureau gave a speech, stating that there are two points to pay attention to: (I) Wuben has a history of 29 years, and it is rare to have such a complete scale in Shanghai. You are fortunate to have the opportunity to study here, and it is hoped that you will pay close attention to your studies and discipline, so as not to disappoint your parents' expectations and the hard work of the municipal authorities in running the school. (II) The founder, Mr. Wu Huaijiu, was so enthusiastic about education two or three decades ago, which is admirable. Now the municipal education expenditure accounts for about a quarter of the total expenditure, and the municipal authorities have more desire to allocate funds to promote women's education, but in fact, it is no longer allowed. It is hoped that there will be more enthusiastic people like Mr. Wu, so that Wuben can be more complete. Then, Ni Wenya gave a speech, stating that it is rare to see Chinese schools with more than 30 years of history, especially girls' schools. Your school has been established for 29 years and is worth commemorating, and it is really worthy. Then, the alumni representative gave a reply, and finally, Principal Wang gave a thank-you speech and the meeting adjourned. From 2:00 PM onwards, there was a recreational performance to celebrate, which was very grand for a time.

Municipal First Field Small Football Tournament to Start Tomorrow 120

Announcing Small Football Information

The Municipal First Public Sports Field Small Football Tournament is scheduled to weigh the height, body length and weight this afternoon, and the competition will start tomorrow morning. It has been reported in the previous newspapers. It is known that the association wants to make the players of each team understand the purpose of the competition and the attitude to be taken during the competition in order to achieve the most satisfactory results, so it publishes small football player information for compliance. The small football player information and the competition schedule for tomorrow are recorded as follows:

Small Football Player Information

(I) You should recognize that the purpose of the competition is not for vanity or trophies, but to connect friendship, learn skills, increase interest in daily practice, and arouse the belief of the audience in the field. (II) You should have a humble attitude and compete with others. Don't be proud if you win, and don't be jealous if you lose. (III) You should have a loving nature. Whether it is a teammate or a teammate of the opposing team, they are always good friends in art. Don't be picky about winning or losing, which will hurt everyone's harmony. (IV) You should have a gentleman's spirit, and never use tricks or deception to win an improper victory. (V) You should have the ability to be independent. During the competition, you should not be disrespectful due to the ridicule, instigation, or disturbances of bystanders. (VI) You should have a strong will, and do not give up arbitrarily or discontinue the competition and withdraw from the association due to setbacks or failures. (VII)

You should have the habit of respecting the referees, and obey and comply with their judgments, whether or not they are satisfactory to me. (VIII) When you arrive at the field for the competition, you should go to the office to sign in. (IX) Before the competition, you should put all the clothes to be changed by the whole team in the bamboo basket prepared by the field and hand them over to the cloakroom for storage. However, do not mix money and valuables in it. (X) In order to save time due to the small number of fields and the large number of teams, there will be a five-minute break in the middle of each game.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 124

— Haike

A male guest (at a banquet of one or two hundred people, speaking to a female guest he doesn't know very well)—Tonight’s banquet is huge. There are a lot of men and women who don’t know each other. I don’t even know the host.

A female guest—Then how did you come, sir?

A male guest—I was dragged here by a friend. But after coming, I felt very regretful. Look at that host. He is a miser of the first rank. How can he entertain guests with such terrible food? Madam, do you know the host?

A female guest—I’m very sorry to say that he is my husband.

Man—My love, I had a dream last night. In the dream, I was proposing to you. I wonder what this foreshadows.

Woman—This is sufficient proof that you are more conscious when you are asleep than when you are awake.

A—I heard you recently moved. What is your new landlord like? Is he a good acquaintance?

B—There’s nothing else wrong with him. It’s a pity that he is too curious. In less than a month, he has already been asking when I will pay the rent. And I happen to be most afraid of this kind of thing.

Father (bursting into the room, seeing his daughter sitting on a young man’s lap)—Oh! This is outrageous! In the past, when I and your mother were in love, we corresponded with each other.

Daughter—Times have changed. Everything is about economy now. Like this, we can save postage on the one hand, and save time writing letters on the other.

Travel Musings in Japan 125

— Cheng Zhizheng

My friend, Mr. Liu Xiaoguang, accompanied Mr. Miao Picheng, the former Director of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department, to Japan for an inspection three months ago. He returned to China yesterday upon completion of his duties. Colleagues from our newspaper hosted a banquet to welcome him back. During the meal, he described the customs of the Japanese islands and shared his observations and feelings, many of which are worth recording. I am thus relaying them here.

The Restoration of Tokyo After the Earthquake: The Tokyo earthquake was the most significant loss in Japanese history, amounting to hundreds of millions. However, visiting the area now, one sees towering buildings and splendid architecture, pleasing to the eye. All aspects of urban construction, such as roads and parks, are even more advanced than before the earthquake. Trying to find remnants of broken tiles and collapsed walls from the earthquake is simply impossible. Moreover, the Japanese, having witnessed the devastation of the earthquake, have built exceptionally sturdy structures in the reconstruction era. Their foresight and perseverance are admirable.

The Passion for Baseball: The Japanese have an unbelievable passion for baseball. One day, during the National Middle School Baseball Tournament, the night before tickets went on sale, the area in front of the stadium was already filled with tents. Spectators, fearing they wouldn't be able to buy tickets, were willing to brave the wind and frost to wait. With so many spectators, those standing further back struggled to see the whole field. As a result, temporary oil drum vendors emerged, charging several yuan to allow spectators to stand on them for a better view. Their business boomed instantly, and they sold out completely. One person, injured in the foot due to the crowd, rushed out of the stadium. After a quick bandage at the hospital, he hurried back. Such fervent enthusiasm is truly rare in the world.

The Diligence and Thrift of Housewives: The Japanese highly value women who manage household affairs and do not engage in external matters. Their frugality is especially commendable. Mr. Liu mentioned seeing a wealthy family with assets of no less than several hundred thousand. Yet, the housewife personally handled the tasks of drawing water and pounding rice, without relying on a single servant. However, she had a unique fondness for flowers and plants. In her garden, there were many pine trees, and she specially hired a renowned craftsman to tend to them, paying him five jiao per day. It took three months to complete the task, costing no less than several hundred yuan.

Public Umbrellas: The Japanese value honesty. Its effectiveness can be seen in the smallest details. In public places, there are often public umbrellas available for loan. When it rains, those without rain gear can take one. After use, they are returned to the original place. It is unheard of for someone to borrow one and not return it.

A Nation Full of Interesting Contradictions: Japan strives to study science but also values its inherent old morals. Therefore, foreigners often see many contradictions. Yet, the Japanese uniquely blend new and old ideas seamlessly, like water and milk. This is truly remarkable. Hence, Westerners often call it an interesting nation.

A Glimpse of the Economic Downturn: The economic downturn in Japan, as reported in newspapers, became even more apparent after arriving there. Major Japanese cities have dozens of department stores, such as Sincere and Wing On. However, upon entering them, one finds few customers and an exceptionally deserted atmosphere. Fear of unemployment is visible everywhere. The government's relief measures consist of lending capital to enable people to make a living or distributing relief goods to prevent people from freezing and starving. However, the effects are minimal. Most amusingly, the unemployed often place a large wooden frame inscribed with their resumes on the main thoroughfare, standing behind the frame, waiting to be hired. This is indeed a pitiful sight.

The Fanatical Worship of the Emperor: The Japanese have immense reverence for the Emperor, treating him as a deity. This is true not only for adults but also for ordinary elementary school students. Mr. Liu visited an elementary school during dismissal time. The students, passing under the Emperor's portrait, all gave the highest salute, solemnly and respectfully. This is truly admirable. One can see the effectiveness of their education.

Tears Flow Uncontrollably at the Sad Reality: Mr. Liu's observations led him to realize that Japan, through diligent effort and vigorous advancement over several decades, has become a wealthy and powerful civilized nation in the world. The training of its people and the establishment of its political system, when compared to our country, make one feel utterly ashamed. During a conversation with someone, he couldn't help but shed tears at the sad reality. The people of our country should know what to strive for!

A Unique Case of Lovers' Suicide 126

— Chen Junshan

The newspaper recently reported that Mr. Liu of Chih Chih College died tragically after being struck by a speeding train while crossing the tracks in front of the school during his lunch break.

Mr. Liu was my close friend. He was gentle, excelled in literature, and was good at socializing. He was particularly close to a certain lady. The shocking news has left me stunned and grief-stricken. Had Mr. Liu not had a deep affection for that lady (who has served as empress), why would he have transferred from the Faculty of Political Science to Far Eastern University? When Far Eastern University closed, he returned to the Faculty of Political Science. Later, upon hearing that the lady had enrolled at Chih Chih College, he transferred to Chih Chih this spring. Three times he moved schools, only to meet this unfortunate end. Alas, what a tragedy!

The Chinese Who Delight in Eating Raw Things 127

— Jiyuyi

The Japanese savage eats raw things. Once, a troupe performed publicly at the Great World entertainment center. Recently, my friend Mr. He came to Shanghai and spoke of the eccentric nature of Snake-catching A-bao from Dongpu, who surpasses even the Japanese savage. I am thus hurrying to record and publish this to entertain the readers.

A-bao, surnamed Chen, learned accounting in his youth. He could identify silver dollars without looking, recognizing them by sound alone. As he grew up, he became rebellious and violent, squandering money without restraint, and eventually dissipating all the family property. As a result, his reputation was ruined, yet he refused to correct his ways and roamed about aimlessly, showing no concern for making a living. His wife died early, leaving behind a daughter, who married and lived alone in a small room. She never spoke of poverty, but her eyesight was sharp, able to discern the finest details in the dark. Therefore, the villagers urged him to work as a night watchman, and after repeated requests, he reluctantly agreed. Dongpu is known for producing wine, and wealthy families all brewed their own. From the moment A-bao became the night watchman, he stayed up all night, the sound of his clapper never ceasing. The wine-making equipment was left out in the open, and he never worried about any loss. Unaccustomed to making a living, he was able to fulfill his duties. This alone is remarkable.

In his sixties, with a dark complexion and squinting eyes, hunched over and fierce-looking, he was still vigorous and active, lurking during the day and coming out at night. He had a lifelong fondness for eating poisonous creatures. Snakes, frogs, spiders, centipedes, geckos, millipedes, and other filthy insects – none escaped his grasp. He would swallow them whole and alive, without washing or chewing. If not, he would barely touch them with his lips and swallow them whole before they died. It only took an instant.

When eating snakes, he would first bite off the head, suck the blood from the neck, and then chew the bones and skin with relish. Larger snakes had to be eaten with sorghum wine, otherwise, half a snake would be enough to fill his stomach. Any more would be too much. People who knew his nature would often tease him with wine, and he would catch snakes from his pocket and perform. This was not just to show off his unique abilities but also because it pleased him.

One year, a Western doctor offered 500 gold coins to buy his body, intending to let him live out his days and then dissect him. The owner of the Great World also heard of his uniqueness and offered a generous sum to hire him to Shanghai, but A-bao refused both times, and it never happened. Moreover, passing by him on a hot, humid day, the foul and strange odor was unbearable. This shows the distinctiveness of his flesh.

Acknowledgement and Introduction: The Yang Brand Machine and Disc Dual-purpose Oil, recently manufactured by Anquan Firm, Weian Lane, Haining Road, this city, is priced at six jiao per bottle. This oil, when dripped into a phonograph, can prevent the machine from experiencing sluggish rotation, uneven speed, and issues such as broken mainsprings and damaged gears. It can also be used to wipe records. We received two bottles as a complimentary gift and hereby acknowledge our thanks and provide an introduction.

Roman Art Observation Notes (V) 128

— Wang Yachen

(1) The Vatican Museum, located next to the current papal palace, is the largest in the world. The Louvre in Paris cannot compare. According to the guide, there are a total of 800 exhibition rooms. Not only is the building vast, but it also houses a wealth of historically renowned artworks. The works of the three great masters of the Renaissance are all found here. Furthermore, there are countless rare ancient sculptures and crafts from around the world. I spent two consecutive days viewing them. Here are my notes on a few important famous paintings.

Upstairs, there are four large Raphael fresco rooms, all with religious themes. Some were painted with the help of his students, but two of them are Raphael's own works. (I've already mentioned Raphael's work above.) There is also the Raphael Gallery, over half a kilometer long, which used to be the residence of the Roman Pope. Raphael gained the Pope's favor by painting this gallery, and it is now named in his memory. Leaving the gallery and going left, there are six large exhibition rooms, all containing modern Italian religious paintings. The techniques lean towards realism, and the colors are bright and vibrant, yet they still maintain the traditions of ancient painting.

(2) The Sistine Chapel: This chapel is famous throughout the world and contains Michelangelo's ceiling paintings and the masterpiece "The Last Judgment." The ceiling painting was started in 1508 and completed in 1522, representing Michelangelo's unparalleled masterpiece. The center of the ceiling depicts events from the creation of the world. The important themes are "The Garden of Eden," "The Expulsion from Paradise," and "The Creation of Mankind," distributed across three sides. Next, it depicts "The Flood," expressing humanity's despair, terror, trembling, anger, violence, sorrow, and other extreme emotions. Furthermore, the depicted God is the embodiment of unlimited natural power, reaching the highest level of sternness. Twenty years after the completion of this painting, he painted the large fresco in the center, another astonishing masterpiece, "The Last Judgment." The original is over ten zhang high and over six zhang wide. Seeing Michelangelo's two great masterpieces together, one can see the difference in style. The ceiling painting is rich in decoration, while "The Last Judgment" emphasizes tension. Everywhere, human tension is used to express divinity. Michelangelo spent seven years on his second masterpiece. The center of the painting is Christ, with Mary on his left and the apostles and martyrs on his right, each carrying instruments of torture and pleading their grievances to Christ. In the upper right, angels come flying in, carrying the cross, and seven angels blow trumpets, resurrecting the dead from their graves, so that everyone can receive the Last Judgment. Some attain eternal happiness, while others are sent to eternal hell. Each part of the painting is full of life. These two large paintings are truly the essence of Renaissance art. Michelangelo had such a great artistic creation that later generations often called him a heroic model of an artist. This is not an exaggeration.

When Michelangelo painted "The Last Judgment," he was greatly influenced by Dante's literature. The lower part of the painting depicts the scene of passengers in a boat about to capsize. The tense expression is all derived from the poetic imagery of Dante.

In addition to the two great masterpieces in the chapel, there are also over ten famous works from the early Renaissance, but due to their high placement, I did not examine them in detail.

The abundance of Roman antiquities cannot be described in a short article. What I have written above is just some of my personal impressions after my visit. The important thing is the focus on art. I will spare further details about other scenic spots and historical aspects.

Warmth in the Heart (301) 129

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Fifteen: Tears Fall All Around, Mourning Crimson Love; A Heart Sways, Lingering Green Intent

Young Master Yin thought secretly, "This time, Gengsheng has fallen into my trap." But when he stepped out of the carriage and looked around, he was a little alarmed. It turned out that this alley was his own property. "Had I known this earlier, I would have come myself. Why bother having Gengsheng lead me here after such a roundabout route? I never imagined that the golden house where Grandpa hides his beauty is actually within my own treasure. It's laughable that we've all been kept in the dark." Following Gengsheng's instructions, he walked into the fifth house in the alley. He saw a sign posted on the door, which read "So-and-so Real Estate Company Office." He thought, "This can't be right. Why is it a real estate company? Could Gengsheng be playing tricks, pointing east while talking west, and fooling me?" He looked at the location of the house and the number on the doorplate and returned to the carriage, saying, "Gengsheng, this isn't right. It's a real estate company. Are you sure you didn't misremember? Isn't it the fifth house?" Gengsheng laughed, "How could I misremember? I come here several times a day. The real estate company is the same as the small mansion, and the small mansion is the same as the real estate company." After all, the young master is clever. He has read detective novels and quickly realized what was going on. He said, "So that real estate company is just a front?" Gengsheng said, "That's not necessarily true. I heard that Uncle Yu and the others originally wanted to establish a real estate company and discussed it with our master. So it was set up there. The concubine lives there alone, and she doesn't need so much space. So the concubine lives on one floor, and the downstairs is used as the real estate company. Fortunately, there's no one in the real estate company. Even when they have meetings, they go elsewhere. All there is is a desk, a mailbox, and a chair, and Master had Mr. Pan, the rent collector from this alley, take care of it. Anyway, it's his own property, so it doesn't cost any money. And it's not convenient to rent the downstairs to someone else, so he set up a real estate company. But in reality, there's no one downstairs. Haven't you noticed that the main door is always closed? If it were a real company, there would be lots of people coming and going. How could the main door stay closed?" The young master thought, "What kind of real estate company is Grandpa running? Is he buying some sort of mobile real estate?" So he asked, "Is this definitely Grandpa's small mansion?" Gengsheng said, "Of course it is. How could I be wrong? I wasn't supposed to bring you to see it. But since Master has already let the cat out of the bag, it's none of my business." The young master said, "I'm afraid you mixed up the house number. When I come back to pick up the concubine, I don't want to end up at the wrong house and cause a scene." "Since it's definitely the right one, then that's settled." So on this day, the young master finally recognized his grandfather's small mansion. At least he accomplished something for his mother. He felt that the two hundred yuan wasn't spent in vain. The mission to investigate was something he could report back on tomorrow. He also repeatedly instructed Gengsheng not to mention it when Master returned. Gengsheng naturally didn't care and wouldn't mention it.

Quietness, Loosening of Money, and Few Foreign Transactions 133

Yarn and Cotton: Initial Rise and Subsequent Stability in the Marked Yarn Market 136

The yarn market initially rose and then stabilized. However, the overseas cotton yarn market tended to rise, slightly exciting the local market. The failure to rise significantly was due to the sluggish sales of current yarn and the lack of activity in various firms, leading to a dispersed atmosphere. With a sufficient supply of goods this month, the market price remained weak. If demand for current yarn can improve, the market may rise.

The Marked Yarn Market is Weak in the Near Term and Strong in the Distant Term. The opening of the marked yarn market was stronger due to the rise in American cotton, with each month rising by 8-9 qian. The market suddenly fell in the second and third sessions due to poor actual sales. As a result, the current month fell by 5 qian, and the distant months rose by 2-4-5-7 qian. The afternoon market was flat, with each month falling by 1-2 qian. The total transaction volume for the day was 21,400 bales. Among the sellers, Da Ji sold 1,250 bales, Yi Cheng sold 1,300 bales, Li Chang sold 1,000 bales, Han Feng sold 1,250 bales, Rong Xing sold 900 bales, and the rest sold 300-400-600-700 bales. Strong Cotton Market Rebound 137
