However, the Han firms sold off slightly. If American cotton can stabilize, the cotton market may rise again.

The Han Standard Rebounded by 5 Qian. The opening of the Han standard market was tense due to the sudden rise in American cotton, and buyers poured in. Each month rose by 3-4 qian, but no one bought the current month, so it was flat. In the afternoon, there were still many buyers, and the market situation was still good. Grains: Rice Market Firm, Weak, and Uneven 140

The market was extremely flat and weak. Late rice arrivals were scarce and sales were stagnant, with no ups or downs. The source of Yangjian rice was depleted, and prices could not be reduced. The general price still opened at 11 yuan and 5-6 jiao. The buying sentiment for Dujian rice was sluggish, and the situation was slightly soft, down 1 jiao. The top price opened at 12 yuan. The stock of customer goods was low, and most of the goods were lost in transit, so the shipments to Shanghai were greatly reduced. Therefore, the market was uniquely firm. The top price for 2 jiao pier rice opened at 11 yuan and 2 jiao. The market for old Baiyuan rice was more active, and high-quality goods were quite tight, opening at 15 yuan and 5 jiao. The buying of Yinyuan standing on consignment was also brisk, and the quoted price was neither high nor low.

In South Shanghai yesterday, over twenty boats arrived at the river, and local sales were flat and normal. The new early rice from regular firms showed a stable state, opening high at 14 yuan and 7 jiao. The digestion of Su Tong Bai rice was sluggish and flat, with only a few scattered inquiries. There were no ups or downs in the market. The stomach for the new thin rice from Nanbang Qingding was slightly active, and store sales were also active. The market price for high-quality goods had to be at 14 yuan. The price of Yang Dujian rice was generally stable, opening high at 10 yuan and 5 jiao. The market for early and late rice here was extremely sluggish and stable. If the sky could be sunny, it would have to be reduced. The range was around 14 yuan and 5 jiao, with no hope of going too low for the time being. The overall trend was quite flat and normal. Yinyuan was similar to the North Shanghai market, with the top price opening at 14 yuan.

Marked Vermicelli Plummets with the Tianjin Market 142

Yesterday, the flour market initially showed stability and then fell. Initially, the quotation of foreign wheat fluctuated very little, and market sentiment was still stable. Later, the Tianjin spot flour market suddenly fell by a huge 8 fen (currently opening at 3 yuan, 3 jiao, and 8 fen) due to reports of sluggish sales and accumulated inventory, as well as the sale of foreign flour by Japanese merchants. This dealt a blow to the initially positive market sentiment. The poor Tianjin market was no different from the excessive rise in Shanghai flour. Later, due to the sharp fall in the current month's standard, insiders and outsiders were inevitably bearish again, and large bulls successively withdrew their positions. Therefore, each month showed an extremely weak and sluggish state. Observing the subsequent steps, if sales do not improve and there are no special changes in foreign wheat, it is feared that the market will fall again. As a result, the current month fell by 1 fen and 7.5 li compared to the previous day, November fell by 1.5 fen, December fell by 1 fen and 7.5 li, January fell by 1.5 fen, and February and March each fell by 1 fen and 7.5 li, it is said.

Near-Term Wheat Plummets by 1.2 Qian 143

Yesterday, the current month's opening price of wheat futures was similar to the previous day. Subsequently, the bulls' thoughts on taking delivery suddenly changed because the market price of the current month differed from November by approximately 2 qian, making it not very worthwhile to take delivery. Moreover, with the slackening of flour sales, flour mills had no appetite. Therefore, almost all positions were returned yesterday, and the stabilized market also immediately shook. The market plummeted, falling by 1.2 qian compared to the previous day's closing price. The large fluctuations were quite alarming. The distant months also slightly weakened, but buying interest was still strong, and the difference in prices was very small. As a result, the current month fell by 1.2 qian compared to the previous day, November fell by 2 fen, December fell by 4 fen, January fell by 3 fen, and February fell by 1 fen. There were no changes in March. The current wheat market showed weakness again. With the sharp fall in the standard, market sentiment softened. Two thousand bags of wheat from Tongsheng, Kaidaoren Bridge, Jiujiang, Suqian, and Zhumadian were on offer. Flour mills took a small portion, and the rest were still in the hands of brokers, it is said.

Grain Exchange Reviews and Approves Foreign Wheat, 144

The Grade Increase Method is a Fatal Blow to Local Wheat

The Grain Exchange, in view of the fact that the quantity of foreign wheat ordered by various factories and firms this year has reached over 100,000 tons, deemed it necessary to review and approve the standard in advance to avoid future confusion. Yesterday, the Wheat Group of the exchange convened all committee members and inspectors to conduct research. However, the issue of upgrading foreign wheat involved significant interests for both bulls and bears, and a heated debate ensued. Those who had contracted foreign wheat naturally argued for an increase in market value, while those who had not contracted were concerned about the source of local wheat and would not allow foreign wheat to overshadow it. It was pointed out on the spot that the weight of the arriving Australian No. 2 wheat was only 144 catties per bag, which was much lower than in previous years. Therefore, a compromise was reached, and it was agreed that Australian large-bag No. 2 wheat would be upgraded by 2.5 qian compared to the standard, small-bag would be upgraded by 2 qian, Canadian No. 3 wheat would be upgraded by 2 qian, and No. 4 wheat would be upgraded by 1 qian. With the agreement of the public, future foreign wheat deliveries will be handled accordingly, which will naturally avoid problems. However, from a factual standpoint, this upgrade poses a great danger to the future of local wheat. The consideration for upgrading foreign wheat is based on the high quality of its goods and its own heavy weight. However, this year, the quality of Shandong Bai wheat is higher than that of foreign wheat, with each stone weighing 150 catties. However, when delivered to the exchange, its due rights are only to increase by 2 grades according to regulations, totaling 6 fen, and after deducting 3 catties of soil, at most 1.6 qian will be upgraded according to the standard. Since the quality and weight are both higher than foreign wheat, the upgrade is less than that of foreign goods, which seems unfair in practice. In addition, as foreign goods sell more and more each day, the main agricultural products are also being suppressed in price for no reason, which is not a blessing for the entire society, it is said.

Local News

Chairman Chiang and Wife Returned to Native Place Yesterday 172

Madam Soong Went East to Recuperate

Chiang and Others Personally Saw Her Off at the Wharf

Chairman Chiang of the National Government, accompanied by his wife, Madam Soong Mei-ling, and more than ten guards, took the Ning Shao Company's Xin Ning Shao ship to Yongbo around 5 p.m. yesterday, transferring to Fenghua, their ancestral home. Prior to this, the military and police authorities, upon Chairman Chiang's instructions, were not permitted to put on a show. Therefore, only a few dozen policemen dispatched by the Public Security Bureau maintained order around the Ning Shao wharf at the 16th Pier temporarily. There were no troops or military bands etc. to add to the spectacle.

Those who went to the wharf yesterday afternoon to see them off included Xiong Shihui, Kong Xiangxi, Yu Qiaqing, Chen Xizeng, Yuan Ludeng, and others. The Shanghai-Ningbo Steamboat Tea Room Workers' Union also hung a banner on the port side of the Xin Ning Shao ship, reading "Welcome Chairman Chiang, who has worked hard and made great contributions, to triumphantly return to his hometown." The Ning Shao Company specially opened up a large first-class cabin for Mr. and Mrs. Chiang, arranging it to be extremely clean. Mr. and Mrs. Chiang arrived at the wharf at 4:40 p.m. yesterday. Madam Soong Mei-ling, together with her elder sister, Ai-ling, first stepped aboard the ship, followed by Chairman Chiang and Minister Kong. Thousands of people swarmed around, vying to catch a glimpse of the Chairman's demeanor. At 5:06 p.m., with a whistle sound, the paddlewheel left the shore.

Chairman Chiang Photographed Aboard the Xin Ning Shao Ship (Photographed by This Newspaper)

Chairman Chiang and Minister Kong Xiangxi and his wife accompanied Madam Soong to the east, taking several cars around 7 a.m. yesterday to escort Madam Soong to the east to Japan to recuperate. After arriving at the Xinguang Wharf, they switched to the Customs Huali small boat and transferred to the Grande President ship of the Da Lai Company. It was not until after 9 a.m. that Chiang and others shook hands with Madam Soong to bid farewell. Those who went to Japan on the same ship to serve her included Soong Zi-an and Minister Kong's youngest daughter, and others. It is said that Madam Soong, following the doctor's instructions, plans to reside in Kobe for recuperation and is scheduled to return home in a month.

After Chairman Chiang and his wife sent Madam Soong to the east, they visited Chen Tiaoyuan, Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, at Quan Jisifei Road around 10 a.m. yesterday, talked for more than ten minutes, and then left. Then they went to Gordon Road to visit Central Committee Member Yu Youren, and returned to the Soong residence at 11 a.m. Those who came to pay respects included Zhang Jingjiang, Chen Mingshu, Chen Tiaoyuan, Huang Yingbai, Qian Xinzhi, Yu Qiaqing, Zhang Qun, Chen Guangfu, and others. At noon, Chiang invited Chen Mingshu, Kong Xiangxi, Ye Zhuotang, Chen Xizeng, and others to lunch at the Cathay Hotel on the Bund. Around 2 p.m., they returned to their residence on Jiaerye Ai Road, and at 4 p.m., they visited Li Shizeng at the Sino-Western Sanatorium on Pushi Road, and then went to the wharf.

Wang Zhengting Discusses Recent Diplomacy 173

Mo Dehui Remains in Russia to Observe the Situation

The German Envoy's Visit Yesterday Had No Mission

Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting met with the German Envoy Büel in the Foreign Affairs Discussion Association on Xiafei Road at ten o'clock yesterday morning, and the German Counselor Belac, the host and guests had a pleasant conversation. After the reporter interviewed the Danish Consul General Long En and others after they resigned, Wang gave an audience and asked about various recent diplomatic issues.

Right: The German Envoy, Center: Foreign Minister Wang (Photographed by This Newspaper) 174

Sino-Russian Negotiations Regarding the Sino-Russian negotiation incident, there is a rumor that Mo Dehui has been recalled to China. Wang replied that although Sino-Russian negotiations have recently stalled, Mo Dehui is still staying in Russia to observe the situation and plan for a response. As for the Boli Conference Record, our side will definitely not recognize it. If Russia insists on using this as a basis, the future is particularly bleak.

Extraterritoriality Regarding the negotiations on the abolition of extraterritoriality, Wang stated that British Envoy Lampson will come to Beijing early next month to continue negotiations. As for the Japanese side, he has repeatedly urged the Japanese Ambassador Shigemitsu Aoi. According to him, he is currently waiting for instructions from the Japanese government and will be able to open discussions once he arrives. Wang also said that French Envoy Weirton will also come south at the beginning of the month to present his credentials and conduct various outstanding cases between China and France.

Diplomatic Entertainment The reporter then asked if the German Envoy's visit this morning had any mission. Wang said that this was an ordinary diplomatic entertainment and had no mission. He was also asked about the issue of Japanese Vice Foreign Minister Nagai's slip of the tongue. Wang made no comment. Foreign Minister Wang hosted a banquet for Belgian Envoy Valoss and his wife at his private residence on Guba Road at eight o'clock last night.

Oppose Japanese Military Drill Attacking Changchun 175

The Authorities Should Protest Seriously

The People Must Rise Up Together to Oppose

｜｜Joint Telegram Issued by Four Branches｜｜

Yesterday's newspaper reported that the Japanese army stationed in the Northeast had the outrageous act of openly practicing attacking Changchun on the 19th of this month. This is truly a great shame to our country and rarely heard in the world. The Japanese imperialists' ambition to invade our country has been completely exposed here. The Ninth, Eighteenth, Twentieth, and Thirtieth Branches of the Third District of this city specially jointly telegraphed the whole country yesterday, requesting the authorities to protest seriously and the people to be aware. The telegram said, "The Japanese imperialists, at a time when the revolutionary atmosphere is permeating the whole country and the domestic warlords are being eliminated one after another, suddenly dared to recklessly practice attacking Changchun, digging trenches and building fortresses, with booming cannons, for three or four hours in the middle of this month in the Northeast of our territory under the pretext of autumn exercises. Their contempt for our sovereignty and insult to our national system have reached their extreme here, and their aggressive ambitions can be further proven here. This kind of strange shame and great humiliation is truly rare in the world and sympathized by the whole country. After the pain and hatred, our branches are determined to deal with it with hot blood. In addition to presenting a serious protest to the diplomatic authorities, we hereby loudly appeal and solemnly declare, hoping that the people of the whole country will unite to oppose it and wash away this strange shame and great humiliation. The party and the country are fortunate. This is a telegram, respectfully printed by the Ninth Branch, the Eighteenth Branch, the Twentieth Branch, and the Thirtieth Branch of the Third District of the Shanghai Special City of the Chinese Kuomintang."

Chen Mingshu Will Not Return to Guangdong for the Time Being 176

Attending the Fourth Plenary Session in Nanjing

This reporter interviewed Chen Mingshu, Chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Government, yesterday and asked about his future whereabouts and whether he would attend the Fourth Plenary Session. He replied that he would stay in Shanghai for a few days and then return to Nanjing temporarily without returning to Guangdong. He would definitely attend the Fourth Plenary Session. He met with Chairman Chiang this morning and discussed matters related to Guangdong.

Jiang Bocheng to Return to Jinan Tomorrow 177

Jiang Bocheng, Chief Staff Officer of the Commander-in-Chief's Camp, previously accompanied Liu Han-hui, the representative of Sun Lianzhong of the Northwest Army, to Beijing to report to Chairman Chiang on the progress of Sun's army's obedience and to request instructions. Then he came to Shanghai the day before yesterday (the 22nd) to rest for a while. Now I know that Jiang has decided to return to Jinan by sea tomorrow due to the importance of Jinan's defense.

Wang Hout and Yesterday Visited Zhang Qun 178

Wang Hout, the acting leader of the consulate stationed in Shanghai and the Consul General of Belgium, went to the Municipal Government at 3 p.m. yesterday to visit Mayor Zhang. Mr. Zhang Qun (right) and Mr. Wang Hout (left) (photographed by this newspaper)

Mr. Zhang Yuejun, accompanied by Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, was invited into the living room and warmly received. It is said that Mr. Wang Hout will take over the duties of leading the consulate as the U.S. Consul General Keginhan returns home. Therefore, yesterday's visit was entirely for the purpose of promoting friendly relations between the countries so that he can contact at any time if there are any incidents in the future.

British Ambassador to Japan, Thelle, Passed Through Shanghai on His Way Home 179

The Shanghai Times reported that British Ambassador to Japan Sir Thelle has requested leave to return home and arrived in Shanghai yesterday (23rd) with his wife and daughter aboard the French mail steamer Isles, staying at the British Consul General Belignan's residence. He will take the original ship to Marseille on Saturday. It is said that the knight may not return to his post after his vacation. As for the successor, the consulate was asked about this yesterday afternoon. It was said that it has not been mentioned at this time. The statement that the current minister to China Sir Lampson will be promoted to the post in Japan is still not confirmed.

Jiangsu Province Pre-Borrows Winter Grain to Slow Repayment 180

The Jiangsu Finance Department has recently received reports from the financial bureau chiefs of 14 counties in Shanghai, including Wujin, Wuxian, Wuxi, and Songjiang, stating that the pre-borrowed winter grain still owes four yuan and five jiao per stone. According to Junling's repayment method, nine jiao of foreign money is allocated for each stone starting from the winter grain in the 19th year until the 23rd year, and all will be returned. Now that the winter grain is about to be collected, they should submit a report for review and follow the instructions, etc. After Chen presented the report, the finance minister said that the budget for this year is still insufficient. If repayments are made, it would be difficult in reality. The Provincial Government Committee decided that the pre-borrowed winter grain should be approved for delayed repayment. The Shanghai County Finance Bureau has been ordered by the Finance Department to comply yesterday.

Request the Government to Promulgate the Patent Law as Soon as Possible 181

Pan Xulun's Proposal at the Industrial and Commercial Conference

Member of the Industrial and Commercial Conference, Accountant Pan Xulun, recently submitted a proposal to the Industrial and Commercial Conference for requesting the government to promulgate the patent law as soon as possible to promote the domestic industry. Those who first invent or specially improve industrial products and manufacturing methods should have the right to patent to encourage them. This is the general practice of various countries. The National Government of our country also promulgated 21 articles of the Provisional Regulations on Encouraging Industrial Products on June 18th of the 17th year, which properly stipulated the procedures for applying for and approving patent rights. Since the implementation of these regulations, many domestic industrialists have followed the regulations to apply and invite approval. This is really the most important step to promote the improvement of industry. However, on July 31st of the 18th year, the National Government issued 7 articles of the Special Industrial Incentive Law and repealed the previously promulgated Provisional Regulations on Encouraging Industrial Products by an edict on April 28th of the 19th year. The government's intention may be that the special manufacturing rights in the Special Industrial Incentive Law can replace the patent rights, but in reality, the special manufacturing rights in the Special Industrial Incentive Law have limited areas, and the term is at most five years. It must be that the industry run by the Chinese people is within the scope listed in the law and has achieved results before it can be applied for. Ordinary patent rights, regardless of Chinese and foreign people, regardless of any industry, can be applied for at the beginning of the invention or improvement to protect and encourage them. Their nature is fundamentally different. Therefore, since the abolition of the Provisional Regulations on Encouraging Industrial Products, according to the experience of Xu Lun personally, there have been many inventors or improvers in the industry who want to apply for patents for their products or methods, but they also suffer from the lack of legal basis and cannot proceed. In the midst of this advocacy of domestic products, the legislative aspect does not seem to be a retrogression. It is proposed that the National Government orders the Legislative Yuan to quickly formulate a special law for the patent rights item to achieve perfection, immediately announce and implement it as an incentive for industrial inventions and improvements. Is it appropriate? I hope the public will decide.

Special Contract Farming Methods of the County Agricultural Education Center 192

The Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center, in order to increase agricultural yields and improve the lives of farmers, has established twenty-four special contract farms. Yesterday, it convened a meeting of farmers and decided on seventeen articles of methods. The crop being tested this year is wheat. Seeds were purchased by the Agricultural Education Center from famous farms in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Staff from the center will provide monthly guidance. The methods are recorded as follows (Special Contract Farming Methods of the Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center): ㈠ This farm will be selected by the center from the relatively nearby farmland of experienced farmers for special testing and will be named the Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center's Number X Special Contract Farm. ㈡ The purpose of this farm is to test and improve crops. The crops to be tested will be determined by the center. ㈢ Each contracted household will farm a maximum of two mu and a minimum of one mu. ㈣ The seeds required for this farm will be provided by the center. ㈤ Contracted farmers should follow the guidance of the center regarding planting and management. They must immediately report any pests or diseases discovered, and the center will devise methods to guide their elimination to prevent major damage and increase yields. ㈥ The harvests from this farm will belong entirely to the contracted farmers. ㈦ The grain tax or land rent for this farm will be paid by the contracted farmers. ㈧ If the experiment fails on this farm, the center will be responsible for compensating the household based on their standard yield for the year. ㈨ Contracted farmers must sell a portion of their agricultural products to the center at the prevailing market price so that they can be promoted annually. ㈩ The center will hold an exhibition after each crop is harvested. Contracted farmers should send their agricultural products to the exhibition, where experts will be hired by the center to evaluate the results, and those with excellent performance will be rewarded. ㈩㈠ Contracted farmers must accurately record the information on the survey forms provided by the center and submit them to the center. ㈩㈡ Contracted farmers will hold a daily meeting convened by the center to discuss various important issues. Special meetings may be held in the event of special circumstances. ㈩㈢ The contract period for the farm is two years, and the contract may not be terminated within the period. ㈩㈣ If a contracted farmer does not comply with the center's plans and guidance, they will be liable for damages. ㈩㈤ The County Public Security Bureau will be requested by the center to protect the contracted farms. ㈩㈥ Contracted farmers have the obligation to guide the farmers in their respective villages. ㈩㈦ Contracted farmers should report any opinions on planting to the center at any time.

Opinions of the Domestic Silk and Satin Industry on the Issue of Account Settlement 193

Wang Xingyi, a standing committee member of the Chinese National Products Preservation Association, recently because the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce regarding the issue of settling accounts using the national calendar, specially recommended five committee members including Wang Yansong to conduct specialized research and properly plan measures, etc. The opinions of the silk and satin industry's business community are now sent to the five committee members in a letter, stating: Respectfully, our association has repeatedly received statements from various industry merchants, factories, and members, claiming that the issue of year-end account settlement, following the national calendar, is extremely important to commercial circulation and should be carefully studied to ensure smooth implementation. Everyone agrees that China is an agricultural country, and the earliness or lateness of store account settlements should be based on agricultural matters. As evidenced by the discussions reported in the newspapers these days regarding the bean and rice industry, the pharmaceutical industry, and the rice milling industry, in the case of the domestic silk and satin industry, there is no problem with when to collect payments for local retail sales. However, for those who specialize in selling to merchant guilds in various provinces, settling accounts at the end of the national calendar year will inevitably create various difficulties. The goods handled by these merchant guilds in Shanghai are transported to those areas and resold, with the majority sold to farmers. They must wait for the harvest of agricultural products before they can exchange them for money to repay the accounts. Now, if we abolish thousands of years of trading habits and issue strict orders at once, it will be difficult to ensure that store accounts are paid off by the end of the national calendar year. Currently, during this period of expensive gold and cheap silver, all commercial sectors are showing signs of decline. This presents an opportunity to develop the domestic goods business. In past years, during the "golden September and silver October" period, it was the peak season for the sales of general merchandise. Unexpectedly, this year's reform of account settlement has led to a sudden change in people's attitudes, with everyone taking a wait-and-see approach. Consequently, the merchant guilds have also become panicked and are sending letters to suspend their business. It is observed that most commercial sectors place emphasis on the winter season. Taking the domestic silk and satin industry as an example, the months of winter and the twelfth lunar month are the peak seasons for the merchant guilds to handle goods for the new year. Therefore, there is a saying that "three seasons are not as good as one winter." If the county magistrate reforms this, it will inevitably cause the loss of the timeliness of handling goods. Not only will businesses have no basis to rely on and suffer extra pain, but the public will also feel that compliance is difficult and be at a loss. The domestic silk and satin industry, at this time of struggling to survive, cannot bear to receive unexpected blows, which would be adding insult to injury. Furthermore, the silver industry associations in the inland counties of Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Wuxi, Danyang, and Wujin have initiated petitions to the provincial government to postpone the account settlement period to the middle of the second month of the next national calendar year. This is truly a good method for understanding the difficulties of businesses and considering the overall business. We believe that merchants and the public are very willing to follow the national calendar, but the issue of commercial account settlement is actually a separate matter that requires careful implementation. Reading the newspapers, we are pleased to learn that you have been commissioned to study the issue of account settlement. We dare not presume to be disrespectful and offer our opinions. We earnestly request that you, based on the opinions of merchants and the public in various regions, and considering all aspects, conduct detailed research and publish your findings as soon as possible to reassure businesses and comply with the situation. We are overwhelmed with public gratitude and await your instructions.

This kind of arrangement clearly disregards the debts and severely damages the reputation of merchants. Based on the aforementioned information, we are hereby requesting your chamber to assist us in urging the shareholders of Wanhe Store to repay the debts owed to Yu Daheng and water carrier Zhou Yutang as soon as possible, in order to protect the merchants' capital. We truly appreciate your public spirit and hope to receive your reply. This letter is addressed to the Datong General Chamber of Commerce.

Request for Improvement of Ash and Soot from the Flour Mill 202

Over a hundred merchants and businesses in Caojiadu Town, including Yong Shengxin Hao, Fengtai Southern Goods Store, Dehe Silver Shop, Xieyu Kerosene Store, Hefeng Kerosene Company, Yifeng Pawnshop, Xiehexiang Foreign Goods Store, Fuchang, Shenda, and two Cigarette Paper Shops, have jointly submitted a petition. The petition states that the town center is a prosperous area, but the Xinji Flour Mill's machinery is running, creating a sound like thunder day and night. Coal ash flies everywhere, making the area extremely dirty. The merchants' goods are soiled, and the residents' health is greatly affected. Furthermore, the townspeople and employees cannot sleep peacefully at night. If this continues, it will not only harm public health but also disturb the peace of the residents. Yesterday, they jointly signed and sealed a petition to the Municipal Government, the Public Security Bureau, and the Social Affairs Bureau, requesting that the mill be ordered to make improvements as soon as possible to maintain the peace of the residents and emphasize hygiene. The text of the petition is recorded below: Petition for the noise and ash of the flour mill to be improved to avoid disturbance to the citizens' peace and health, etc. The Xinji Flour Mill is located in the center of the bustling Caojiadu area. Previously, when the mill was named Lida Flour Mill, it burned bituminous coal, and the ash was discharged from the basement. The machinery's noise was very low. Now, the mill has been renamed Xinji and reopened. The machinery uses diesel fuel, and when the engine starts, the sound is like thunder, and the houses shake. The noise can be heard far and wide. In addition, the ash and soot are not discharged from the basement but are emitted directly into the sky, flying everywhere. The surrounding residents and businesses are enveloped in smoke and smog, day and night. Hundreds of households and shops nearby cannot keep their homes clean during the day and cannot sleep peacefully at night. The laborers and residents are suffering unimaginable hardships. This matter involves public nuisance. Reluctantly, we have presented the true situation and jointly signed and sealed this petition. We earnestly request that you investigate and verify this matter and order the mill to make improvements to maintain the peace of the residents and emphasize public health. We await your instructions with utmost respect.

More Local News on the Following Page 204

Page 15

Local News Two

Wife of Yang Shuding, Manager of Jiaotong Bank Office, Kidnapped 205

Encountered Bandits on the Way Back from a Funeral

Coachman Bleeding from a Head Wound

Everyone Forced Out of Ten Vehicles

Yang's Wife Immediately Abducted

At 9:45 last night, four bandits kidnapped Mrs. Ren, the wife of Yang Shuding, the manager of the first office of Jiaotong Bank, on the south side of Nanchengdu Road and Weihaiwei Road. They used guns to force Yang's daughter, a maid, a tutor, a coachman, and others out of the car, and then drove off in Yang's own automobile, license number 8995. The results of the investigation are recorded below:

Yang's Wife Attended Funeral of Eldest Brother

Yang Shuding of Jiaotong Bank lives at No. 30 Nikelu Road. His wife, Ren, is from Suzhou and is 32 years old. Yesterday was the 21st day after her husband's older brother's death. Ren, out of consideration for her husband's brother, personally took her eldest daughter, a maid, and a tutor, and ordered the coachman Ah Chun to drive her husband's own automobile, license number 995, to Yang's residence on Nanchengdu Road to attend the funeral.

Encountered Bandits on the Way Home

At 9:45 last night, Yang Ren, because the funeral ceremony at her elder brother's house had ended, ordered the coachman to prepare after dinner. She ordered her daughter, maid, and tutor to board the car, intending to go home to sleep. Unexpectedly, when the car reached the south side of Nanchengdu Road and Weihaiwei Road, four bandits suddenly appeared. Two of the bandits, armed with handguns, approached Yang Ren's car, ordered the coachman to stop the engine, and threatened him with guns.

Tutor's Soul Flew Out of His Body

At that time, Yang Ren, her daughter, and the maid sitting in the car were all women. They trembled with fear at the sight of the situation. The tutor, Mr. Someone, an old scholar, was also panicked by the situation. The coachman, Ah Chun, was still trying to turn on the engine and drive away. The bandits, without mercy, struck through the window with a gun butt. The glass shattered and flew everywhere, and the coachman's face was covered in blood as a result.

Four Bandits Kidnapped People and Took the Car

Seeing that the coachman could no longer resist, the bandits immediately opened the car door. Two bandits dragged out Yang's daughter and the maid. Two bandits used guns to order the coachman and the tutor to get out of the car. Everyone was faced with a dangerous situation. It was also drizzling lightly, the street lights were dim, and there was no way to call for help. They had no choice but to let the bandits do what they wanted. Seeing that their purpose had been achieved, the four bandits boarded the car. One of the bandits started the engine and drove the people and the car north.

Police Station Found No Trace

Yang's coachman and others saw their mistress being kidnapped and were unable to rescue her. They hired a streetcar and went to the Xinzha police station to report the incident. Upon hearing the news, the head of the police questioned the coachman about the situation and ordered the detectives to rush to the scene to investigate. He also informed all the police stations to assist in the search. The police stations in the Chinese and French Concessions were notified to pay attention to car number 8995. At the time of the reporter's writing, the car had not yet been found.

Da Xia Student Yuan Shunwu Abducted 206

Yuan Shunwu's cries for help were futile

A coughing rickshaw puller gets slapped

Yuan Shunwu, a sophomore majoring in commerce at Da Xia University on Zhongshan Road, finished his dinner at the Lu Zhong Western Restaurant opposite the school gate at around 6:30 PM yesterday. As he was walking back to school along Zhongshan Road, he was suddenly forced into a pre-arranged car by a group of kidnappers and driven north. Because the area falls under the jurisdiction of the Sixth District, the student union dispatched Shi Zhaoyuan to report Yuan Shunwu's abduction to the Sixth District General Office and request an investigation. Upon receiving the report, District Chief Ren immediately ordered all armed personnel and police stations to conduct separate investigations. As of 11 PM, there were still no leads. The details of the abduction are as follows:

The kidnappers hired a car. At 5:15 PM yesterday, two men, one wearing a white-gray long gown and the other a black long gown, both around 30 years old and speaking with a northern accent, rented a car from You Ning Car Company at the intersection of Xizang Road and Shantou Road. They identified themselves as surnamed Liu. The accountant signed a Chinese settlement certificate numbered 4417 and a concession certificate numbered 18055 for a Chevrolet sedan. The chauffeur, Zhu Xingtang, drove the car. The man in the black gown sat in the front, and the man in the white gown sat in the back. When the chauffeur asked where they were going, the kidnappers said they were going to Zhabei. As the car passed the northern end of the Xin Zha Bridge, the kidnappers ordered the car to stop. The man in the back got out of the car and ordered the chauffeur to drive to a quieter place on Gonghe Xin Road, where they stopped next to what appeared to be a guild hall. Three more men got into the car. Two were wearing long gowns, one black and one white-gray, and the other was wearing a black short outfit. After the three men got in, they ordered the car to drive to Caojiadu via Zhongshan Road. They ordered the car to stop intermittently. On the way back, two more men suddenly appeared, one in a white-gray long gown and the other in a short outfit. They pointed a pistol at the chauffeur and said, "Get out. Sorry, we need to borrow the car." After the chauffeur got out of the car, he was dragged by the two kidnappers to a grassy area in a nearby cemetery and guarded. The remaining kidnappers drove the car south.

The chauffeur was slapped. The chauffeur was dragged into the grassy area by the two kidnappers, who ordered him to sit down and forbade him from making any noise. The chauffeur coughed once because he was out of breath. One of the kidnappers immediately slapped him forcefully and said, "Don't you dare make a sound, understand?" After sitting quietly in the grassy area for about an hour, it started to drizzle. The kidnappers finally said, "You can go back now." The two kidnappers then strode off to the north. The chauffeur walked south along Zhongshan Road for about 20 minutes before reaching Da Xia University. He asked someone where the police station was and recounted what had happened. Only then did he learn that the men who borrowed the car had come to kidnap a Da Xia student. Someone hired a rickshaw to take him to the Sixth District General Office to report the incident.

Circumstances of the Abduction: Yuan Shunwu walked out of the restaurant with two roommates (from Qunli Zhai, No. 237), Yu Deyuan and Chen Xianhe, side by side, chatting and laughing. Unexpectedly, as they walked along Zhongshan Road, they suddenly saw a car making a U-turn from south to north. The door was not closed. At the same time, someone holding a flashlight shone it in the faces of the three men. A kidnapper holding a pistol stepped forward and forced Yuan Shunwu into the car, which sped off to the north. When Yuan Shunwu was forced into the car, Chen and Yu were unable to rescue him. They only heard Yuan Shunwu shouting for help, but he seemed to have been gagged by the kidnappers, so they heard no further sound.

Yuan's Family Situation: According to Yuan Shunwu's fellow villager and classmate, Ye Yuan, Mr. Yuan is from Wuchang, Hubei. He is 19 years old this year and lives in Hankou. His father runs the Yuan Ruitai Construction Factory in Hankou. On the surface, it seems to be doing well, but in reality, it is not. Mr. Yuan is studying commerce and is currently in his second year. He has no family in Shanghai. This abduction may be a case of mistaken identity because Mr. Yuan is not actually qualified to be kidnapped. Furthermore, Mr. Yuan seems to suffer from neurasthenia. Yesterday afternoon, around 4 PM, he and Ye Yuan took the school's public car to Datong Road to consult a doctor.

Police Station's Vigorous Pursuit: After this incident occurred, the Da Xia Student Union dispatched student Shi Zhaoyuan, carrying a recent photo of Mr. Yuan, to report the incident to the Sixth District General Office and request a thorough investigation. At the same time, chauffeur Zhu Xingtang also went to the district to report the kidnappers' car rental. Upon receiving the report, Director Ren, considering the incident occurred within his jurisdiction and involved a staff member, immediately personally ordered Inspector Xu to lead the patrol squad and the entire detective team, fully armed, to search everywhere. He also ordered all police stations to pay attention and notified the Fourth District General Office, requesting them to order their subordinates to cooperate in the investigation. When the reporter arrived at the Sixth District General Office, Director Ren and Inspector Xu had already returned to the General Office and were studying investigation methods and deployment plans.

Water Patrol Captain Shelters Opium Traffickers Discovered 207

Both People and Goods Seized

Escorted to the Local Court for Interrogation

Xu Yan, the acting captain of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau's Water Patrol Team, recently apprehended two opium traffickers, Shen and Zhou, as well as a boat owner named Zhou Fucheng, totaling 3,816 taels of opium, divided into five bundles. Xu Yan colluded with patrol police Jiang Shihe, detectives Ma Zhiyun, Zhang Longfa, and others to accept a bribe of 1,300 yuan, released the opium traffickers, and embezzled all the opium, hiding it under the deck of the Water Patrol Team's boat, intending to sell it for profit. Unexpectedly, someone informed on them. Director Yuan, greatly angered, cited the National Government's law that officials who embezzle more than 1,000 yuan are to be sentenced to death according to the law. Yet they dared to try this and even dared to embezzle opium, which is contrary to the anti-smoking law. Therefore, he immediately dispatched an inspector to arrest boat owner Zhou Fucheng. After questioning him and learning the truth and the location of the opium, the inspector rushed to the Water Patrol Team, searched out the stolen opium, and detained Xu Yan and Jiang Shihe. Ma Zhiyun and Zhang Longfa had already fled. Immediately, both people and goods were escorted to the bureau. Director Yuan interrogated them, and they all confessed. Yesterday, Director Yuan prepared official letters and sent police to escort Xu Yan, Jiang Shihe, and Zhou Fucheng to the local court at 4 PM, requesting a severe punishment. After the preliminary examination by the prosecutor, they were ordered to be detained pending further proceedings.

Thief Escapes While Handcuffed 208

Xie Aofu cuts open the handcuffs for him

Caught in the act by a detective, punished

The day before yesterday afternoon, Wang Zitang, a native of Anhui, stole a small clock in the Chinese area of Zhabei. A police officer saw this and detained Wang in the Fourth District General Office of the Public Security Bureau. After interrogation, he was ordered to be sent to the Beggar Education Institute for training. The bailiff handcuffed Wang's hands and hired two rickshaws. Wang was in front, and the police were behind. While passing Gonghe Xin Road, Wang seized the opportunity to jump out of the rickshaw and run away. He disappeared immediately. The police officer could not catch up and had to return to the station to report and conduct a strict search. At 8:30 PM that evening, Wang entered North Shansi Road in the Public Concession and was seen by Xie Aofu, a native of Changzhou. Because his hands were handcuffed, he was questioned. Wang confessed the truth. Xie then borrowed a file from the Dexing Copper Shop, opened by Lin Xinyao, a Ningbo native, at No. 183 in a nearby alley, and used the file to cut off one of Wang's handcuffs at the back door of the shop. While he was cutting the second handcuff, he was seen by a colleague of Shang Wu, a Chinese detective of the Huishi Patrol Room. He reported to Detective Shang and went with a Western detective to arrest Wang Zitang and Xie Aofu. Together with the owner of the Dexing Copper Shop, Lin Xinyao, the handcuffs, and the file, they were taken to the patrol room for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the Special District Local Court. Wang Yaotang, the patrol room's lawyer, stood up and presented the case, stating that Wang Zitang should be transferred to the Branch Security Bureau for interrogation. For Xie and Lin, the patrol room accused them of assisting in the escape and requested that they be punished according to the law. Detective Xu also testified that he witnessed the defendant Xie Aoxuan cutting off Wang's handcuffs with a file. However, the shop owner Lin Xinyao did not see it. Wang Zitang also confessed to how he escaped and Xie cut off his handcuffs. When Xie and Lin were questioned, their statements were evasive. After verifying the confession, Judge Wu Tingqi sentenced Xie to six months in prison, found Lin not guilty, and transferred Wang Zitang to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Municipal Bureau of Public Works Addresses Dangerous Old Houses 210

There are dilapidated and leaning houses everywhere in this city, especially in the Chinese area. Most of these old houses have rotten pillars and leaning walls, and danger can occur at any time. In recent years, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works has repeatedly selected the most dangerous ones for rectification. Therefore, the dilapidated houses that used to catch our eyes in the Nanshi and Zhabei areas have now been gradually rebuilt, appearing cleaner. After the roads have been widened, traffic is also more convenient. However, generally, people do not believe the danger until the house collapses. When it really collapses, they complain. Therefore, enforcing rectification is not easy. It is said that the Municipal Bureau of Public Works has always been cautious in addressing dangerous houses. Whether the report comes from citizens or the bureau's surveyors, they will send personnel to re-inspect and verify in detail before deciding on rectification. A photo is taken to record the situation before deciding on rectification, and then the owner is notified to dismantle the house based on the dangerous situation, to fulfill the responsibility of advising. The Municipal Bureau of Public Works recently submitted a list of dangerous old houses to the municipal government for demolition within a time limit (omitted).

Municipal Bureau of Public Works Prevents Impersonation of Surveying Engineers 211

The Municipal Bureau of Public Works recently issued a notice to citizens to pay attention to the discovery of unscrupulous individuals in the city who impersonate surveying engineers to swindle and deceive. In the future, if such incidents occur, they should report to the bureau at any time for thorough investigation. The original text of the announcement is as follows: It is hereby announced that recently, it has been heard that unscrupulous individuals have repeatedly impersonated surveying engineers of this bureau to swindle and extort money. Not only are citizens disturbed by them, but also the reputation of this bureau is affected, which is regrettable. All staff members of this bureau have been issued staff cards, which they carry with them. A photo of the staff member is affixed to the card, making it easy to identify. As for surveying engineers, because they are in charge of fieldwork, a shield-shaped survey card is issued in addition to the staff card to show solemnity and for identification. Citizens, if they encounter these surveying personnel, may check their credentials at any time. If they find that they are not wearing a survey card or have no staff card, or if they have a card but the person and photo do not match, they must be impersonating and can be arrested and prosecuted. Those who did not notice it beforehand and were deceived should also report the facts to this bureau afterward for investigation and punishment. However, most citizens are aware that they are willing to be fooled at the beginning when they encounter such incidents. When they discover that they have been deceived, they are afraid of causing trouble and are unwilling to come forward to report it, so that this bureau cannot see everything and remove this pest from society. This is regrettable. It should be known that the government and the citizens are one body. Without a spirit of mutual assistance and cooperation, the government, despite having the heart to eliminate evil, will be difficult to thoroughly clean up the mess. This announcement is made for everyone to know. In the future, when dealing with this bureau, be sure to come to the bureau in person and do not entrust it to others. If any deception still occurs, you must report the facts to the bureau at any time for thorough investigation. This bureau has high hopes for this.

Ford Airplane Arrives in Shanghai Today 212

The Ford three-motor high-wing monoplane, which took off from Liaoning on the 21st, arrived safely in Tianjin. The pilots, Mr. Priheredden and Mr. Kriesden, gave a test flight to various circles in Tianjin and will set off for Shanghai soon. It may stop briefly in Jinan en route. If the weather is favorable, it will arrive in Shanghai at 4:30 PM today and land at Hongqiao Airport. This is one of the various Ford airplanes, the same type as the airplane that Admiral Byrd rode in the "South Pole Expedition" film recently shown in various movie theaters in Shanghai. The entire plane is made of newly invented alloy, which is strong, light, fireproof, and stainless. It is equipped with three motors, and it can fly with only two of them running. The two wings are high-wing monoplane type, and the passengers have a very wide view. There is a toilet and a luggage compartment. It is said that it will stay in Shanghai for a short time and invite people from all walks of life to try it out, and then fly to Hong Kong and Guangzhou.

Russian Rafalov Commits Suicide 218

The North China Daily News reported that at 1 PM yesterday, a Russian named Rafalov committed suicide with a gun inside Hexuecui Da Xia. Mr. Rafalov came to China three years ago, initially as a journalist. He was once associated with two White Russian newspapers in Shanghai. Later, he went to Harbin as a reporter for the news agency and editor of the Tianjin Russian Weekly. In May this year, he returned to Shanghai and left the journalistic profession. At about 1 PM yesterday afternoon, his wife entered the room and was shocked to see Mr. Rafalov lying stiffly in a pool of blood with a bullet hole in his forehead. Another Browning pistol was abandoned beside him. Before shooting himself, he had apparently taken poison first. His body was immediately taken to the American Funeral Home and will be buried today (24th). It is said that Mr. Rafalov belonged to the Trotsky faction of the Communist Party. Three years ago, when Trotsky fell out of favor and was forced to leave the country, his real name was Bobushkin. He has a sister, who is the wife of Rykov, Chairman of the Council of People's Commissars of the Soviet Union. Therefore, he was well-known among Russian expatriates. According to the Ta Mei Evening News, Mr. Rafalov committed suicide because he lost a lot of money in gambling.

Private Arms Trafficking Case Awaiting Further Interrogation 219

At 9:30 AM yesterday morning, Chen Qingyuan, a native of Shantou, hid a large number of arms in the interlayer of kerosene tanks and the bottom of shoe baskets. He hired a small car to transport them to the Yihua Wharf on Yuanfang Road in Hongkou, intending to transport them to Shantou by boat for profit. Detective Ding Yugao and Western detective of the Hongkou Patrol Room learned of this and went to the wharf, arrested Chen, and took Zhou Zicheng, two kerosene tanks, and a shoe basket to the patrol room. Four pistols were found in the bottom of the shoe basket. The kerosene tanks were opened, filled with sesame oil, with interlayers on both sides. Six Mauser pistols, one pistol, 475 bullets, five bullet boxes, and a spring were found. According to Chen's confession, the arms were purchased from a certain Japanese at No. 121 Peng Road and Lin Xinrui, a Ningbo native at No. 912 Broadway Road. The detectives went to arrest the Japanese and Lin one after another, and also brought Wang Yun, a native of Haizhou, and Yu Shixian, a native of Qingkou, to the patrol room. The Japanese was transferred to the Japanese Consulate for interrogation. Chen and the other five people were detained separately pending escort to the Special District Court for interrogation.

Zhu and Zhang Remanded Pending Sentencing

Xu Zide, the young owner of Shunxing Niupihao at No. 229 Diswei Road, was invited by Zhu Shunjin, a fellow trade native of Anhui, to visit the Wing On Company in June this year and fell in love with Zhang Naizhen, a local hostess. He successively used 1,968 yuan from the business. The case was reported by his father, Xu Yuhe, to the Hongkou Patrol Room, and detectives Chen Baozhong arrested Zhu and Ms. Zhang and escorted them to the Special District Court. Xu Zide was ordered to provide a shop guarantee that he would be available at any time, Zhang Naizhen was ordered to provide a 1,000 yuan shop guarantee, and Zhu Shunjin was remanded. The Wing On Company hostesses Afang and Aifeng were summoned to court to verify the situation, which has been reported in this newspaper. Ms. Zhang was detained in the women's prison without bail. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide continued the trial in the Third Criminal Court. Attorney Li Zhishan of the patrol room stated that the change of date was in progress. The patrol room sent detectives to the Wing On Company playground to investigate the two hostesses Afang and Aifeng. According to the staff of the department, the two women had not been in service successively between the 12th and 16th of this month. Their home addresses are unknown. Now there are two hotel teahouse servants who came to court to testify, please inquire. Lin Shude, a teahouse servant at the New World Hotel, said that the defendant Xu Zide came in June, opened a room, a total of four times. Zhu Shunjin and a woman, Zhang Naizhen, arrived one after another each time. The second time, Xu, Zhu, Ms. Zhang, and another woman gathered in the room to play mahjong. Later, Xu and Ms. Zhang slept in the same room, and Zhu only stayed one night. As to the relationship between Xu and Ms. Zhang, I did not know because it was inconvenient to ask. However, all accommodation costs were paid by Xu, etc. Hu Huasheng, a teahouse servant at the Far East Hotel, also said that Xu Zide and Ms. Zhang came to open a room from the 2nd to the 15th of this month, a total of three times. Zhu was also there in the evening. Ms. Zhang and Xu stayed together for two nights. When questioned, Xu Zide confessed that I went to the Wing On Company and fell in love with Ms. Zhang. Zhu invited me to introduce her. The funds that were lost in the business were also instigated by Zhu. He successively gave Ms. Zhang money to buy clothes and lent Zhu 60 yuan. I and Ms. Zhang did go to the New World Hotel, the Far East Hotel, and the Central Hotel and slept together for several nights. Patrol Attorney Li then stood up and asked Xu, why did you not confess the words you confessed just now during the last court hearing? Xu said that when I was detained in the patrol room, Zhu threatened me and did not allow me to speak frankly, otherwise he would put me to death in the future, so I did not speak frankly. Zhu Shunjin firmly stated that Xu went to Wing On to play and opened rooms in various hotels, etc. were all done by Xu himself, not instigated by me. However, I borrowed 60 yuan from Xu, but I also used more than 200 yuan for traveling with Xu for several months, etc. When Zhang Naizhen was questioned, she said that Xu Zide came to the company to play tea three times, and gave me a gold watch. Later, she became close to hostess No. 3, Afang. What he said in court today deliberately framed me, etc. Judge Feng verified the confession, ordered the lawyers on both sides to debate, and then ordered Xu to return the original guarantee, and Zhu Shunjin and Zhang Naizhen were remanded to wait for a scheduled sentence.

Gu Aqings Implication Case Heard Yesterday 221

Gu Aqing, also known as Gu Ziqing/Gu Cheng, was previously suspected of kidnapping and was detained by Chief Inspector Xie Shuiquan, Detective Ma Xiaozhi, and Detective Jin Guanya of the General Patrol Room and escorted to the Special District Local Court for interrogation. It is reported that the patrol room, in order to comply with the order of the court last time, should submit any evidence that is beneficial to the defendant within the period of change of date for nuclear debate at any time, so Gu was escorted to the First Criminal Court of Shi Te yesterday morning. Judge Sun Yuan and Prosecutor Xu Mei sat in the seat for questioning. Patrol Attorney Ru Baozhen said that during the period of change of date, evidence that was beneficial to Gu was found, but there are still suspicions. For the sake of fairness, the patrol room brought the defendant to court and ordered him to pay bail, but the minimum amount of bail is 10,000 yuan. If the court thinks it is still light, the bail can be increased again. There is one more point that should be noted, that is, the defendant previously claimed to be a shareholder of Daming Glasses Company. Now the patrol room has received a formal letter from Daming, denying that there is a Mr. Gu among the shareholders of the company. The patrol room has verified that the defendant opened the Shanghai Glasses Company in Dalian, which caused this misunderstanding. Yuan Yang'an, the defendant's lawyer, stated that the defendant really has nothing to do with this case and is a legitimate businessman who has invested a lot in the industrial sector. Shenzhou Hotel also has capital of 25,000 yuan. This time, he was really wronged and requested to be released. Even if he is suspected, please allow him to provide a common guarantee that he will be available at any time, because the defendant has a lot of assets and will never abscond. Attorney Ru replied that this is a serious kidnapping case, not a trivial case that can be compared to. If a common guarantee can be provided for a kidnapping case, then no guarantee will be required for other cases. After Judge Sun Yuan slightly questioned the defendant, he announced that the date of the trial is near, and if the defendant provides bail and goes out, it will hinder the patrol room's investigation. Therefore, the request for bail cannot be approved. The defendant was remanded.

The Wife and Daughter of Liu Yingzhou Have Not Yet Been Buried 222

The case of the double suicide by hanging of Liu Zhou, the wife of Liu Yingzhou of No. 5 Maoxingfang, Fumin Road, and her twelve-year-old daughter Yun'e, resulted in Liu Yingzhou being detained by Prosecutor Wu after questioning. However, Liu Yingzhou, who is seen as the catalyst, had filed a lawsuit seeking to live separately from his wife. Yesterday morning was the court date, but Liu was detained, and his lawyer, Shen Yong, also failed to appear. The prosecutor instructed that the two bodies should be collected and buried by Liu Yingzhou's father, but as of yesterday, they had not yet been buried. Therefore, Zhou Qifeng, the brother of the deceased, reported to the court again. The court ordered the local head to find Liu's father to arrange the burial, or else he would be prosecuted.

Brawl During Prostitution Attempt Leads to Assault 223

Sun Yuanlan, a 47-year-old man from Ningbo, works as a mechanic at the Yangshupu Tram Depot. Together with Wang Shifa (30 years old), a coppersmith from the same factory, he went to the home of a widowed woman surnamed Wu at No. 1, West Lane, Weixingli, Taopeng Road, to solicit prostitution the night before last. Two others were with them, one nicknamed "Gaoliang Bottle" and the other named Debiao, both unemployed vagrants. As the tenth round was about to end, Debiao had lost some money. Just as Sun dealt a card with two sixes and one, he called out "yao ding." Debiao then said "yao ding wants to eat," and a conflict arose between them in their speech, leading to a fight. They were separated by others, and agreed to meet at a tea house on Pingliang Road yesterday afternoon to talk things over. When the time came, Sun and Wang, not willing to be outdone, went on time. During the argument, Debiao insisted that Sun pay him twenty yuan to settle the matter, but Sun retorted. Debiao then gathered a crowd to attack Yuanlan with knives, cutting his right leg, causing profuse bleeding. They also used an iron ruler to injure Wang's back. When patrol officers No. 2430 arrived after hearing the news, the assailants had already disappeared. The two injured men were sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment. The patrol officers reported to the head officer to apprehend the criminals for severe punishment.

Theft of a Shipment of Hair 224

The Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Public Transit Company shipped seven pieces of hair from Hangzhou the day before yesterday. The freight car arrived at the South Station for unloading. Because the goods could not be stored in the warehouse, they could only be piled outside the station. That night, one piece, weighing more than fifty pounds, was stolen. The company reported to the guild, and a letter was sent to the railway police department, requesting them to send detectives to investigate and strictly apprehend the culprits.

Chauffeur Fight 225

Due to a love triangle dispute

The perpetrator has fled without a trace

Qian Fulian, a chauffeur from Wuxi, working for Deng Peizeng at No. 16, Dachongli, No. 246 Tongfu Road, is 27 years old. He usually arrives early and leaves late, and has been working for only a month. Yesterday morning at nine o'clock, chauffeur Fulin was having breakfast when suddenly a woman and a man came to Deng's back door looking for Fulin. At that time, the maid, Peng, happened to open the back door and, seeing that they were looking for Fulin, she turned around to inform him. Fulin, hearing the news, stopped eating and went outside. Unexpectedly, the visitors spoke to him in a harsh tone. First, there was a verbal argument, and then the man punched Fulin in the chest. Fulin immediately fought back, and the two began to fight. The man then pulled out a knife from his pocket and stabbed Fulin in the leg, penetrating deeply, causing a gush of blood. The woman, seeing this, became very alarmed and scolded the man for doing so, saying she would rather be stabbed to death instead. After speaking, she threw the knife into Yonglifang in the next alley, and tried to comfort Fulin. At that time, there was a lot of noise in Dachongli, and blood was everywhere. The assailant, seeing that his goal had been achieved, fled without a trace in the confusion. Later, a patrol officer arrived and took the injured man to Baolong Hospital for treatment, and took the woman to the police station, where she will be interrogated today. According to a reporter's investigation, the woman who came with the assailant was Fulin's mistress. This time, because Fulin had rejected her, she had become acquainted with another man. Yesterday's visit was nothing more than an attempt to negotiate with Fulin, but unexpectedly it turned into this violent act.

Woman Petitions for Division of Inheritance 226

Zhu Guibao, a local woman, is 29 years old. Her father, Zhu Yatou, passed away when she was only five years old, and her sister was still an infant. Her father left behind a considerable amount of property, such as the land where the Tiandechi Bathhouse is located on Rue Cardinal Fesch in the French Concession, and the land behind the Tiandechi old house, along with the houses and two adjacent plots of old house land, and fifteen Japanese-style houses on the land. Also, the Hongqiao Cemetery on Route Paul Beau, totaling more than ten mu of land and houses, is of considerable value, all of which has been occupied by her cousins Zhu Shengquan, Zhu Jinhua, and Zhu Kunhua. Although she has repeatedly asked Shengquan and others for a division, they have ignored her. Zhu Yatou, the father of Guibao, and Zhu Siyuan, the father of Zhu Shengquan, were brothers. All the property was jointly owned by the three siblings. Since the promulgation of the women's inheritance law by the National Government, Guibao has also asked relatives to ask Shengquan for a fair division (all the property is managed by Shengquan), but he has refused to reason. Therefore, Guibao had no choice but to hire lawyer Jin Yu to file a complaint with the court, arguing for the retroactive application of the women's inheritance law, demanding an equal division, in accordance with the law. The court has accepted the case and issued a summons.

Investigating Beef and Mutton Restaurants 227

Preparing for Inspection and Crackdown

The beef, mutton, and pork sold by the meat shops in this city must be inspected by the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau's official doctors beforehand. The cattle, sheep, and pigs must be healthy before they can be sent to the public slaughterhouse for slaughter and stamping, and then sent to the meat shops for retail sale. The crackdown is quite strict. Now, the Health Bureau has found that the mutton sold by the religious halls (i.e., Muslim halls) and mutton restaurants in the city is not sent for inspection beforehand, nor is it slaughtered and stamped in the designated public slaughterhouse. Whether the quality of the meat sold is clean or not is a matter of hygiene. A letter has been sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, ordering each district to investigate the number of religious halls and mutton restaurants within its jurisdiction, to copy the names and addresses of the owners, and to reply to the bureau, so that personnel can be sent to inspect and strictly crack down on them, in order to emphasize hygiene.

Accusations of Enticing Two Young Women 228

Fei Qiu, a woman residing in a small room at No. 146 Caishi Street in the French Concession, reported to the French police the other day that her husband's younger sisters, namely the woman's nieces Fei Guirong, 18, and Fei Xiaomao, 17, had been living with the woman. Unexpectedly, the other day, Bao Jianrong, who lived on the third floor of the same building, and his wife, Zhu, colluded to entice the two young women to hide in the Dalu Restaurant in Sanmaoge Bridge, with improper intentions. She requested that the case be investigated. The police chief approved the request and immediately ordered detective Hang Guangfu to bring Bao and his wife, together with the two women, to the police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the French court for questioning. First, the plaintiff, Fei Qiu, complained about the circumstances of the abduction. Then, Fei Guirong and Fei Xiaomao both stated that the defendants had enticed the women to the hotel and held them in confinement, saying that the women had no way out living with their sister-in-law, and that they should follow them to Shanghai to work in a "swallow's nest" (brothel). If they were not good at it, they could go to other cities to work, where they could earn at least sixty or seventy yuan a month. Bao Jianrong and his wife both claimed that they were in the foreign goods business, but because business was slow, they had accumulated a lot of debt. So, with the help of friends, they opened a room in the Dalu Restaurant to gamble and skim profits, hoping to pay off their debts. As for the Guirong and Xiaomao sisters, they voluntarily went to the hotel to play with them, and their sister-in-law had agreed to it beforehand. They dared not engage in any illegal activities, and requested a clear investigation. Judge Zhu Cheng ordered the two defendants to be remanded in custody, pending the police investigation to determine whether the plaintiff knew about it beforehand, before making a final decision.

Stealing Crabs in the Season of Autumn's High Sky and Fat Crabs 229

Chen Zhaorong Arrested for Snatching Crabs

Shi Xueyi, a native of Tongzhou, residing at No. 15 Hubei Alley, Old Baidu, Pudong, is 35 years old and has always made a living by farming. A few days ago, Shi returned to his hometown on business. Yesterday, he took a boat back to Shanghai. As it was the season for fresh crabs, he bought a basket of large crabs, about eighty in total, in Tongzhou. At about 1:00 PM, the boat arrived at the wharf and docked at Wangjia Wharf in Nanshi. Shi carried the crab basket ashore and was about to hire a sampan to return to Pudong when Chen Zhaorong, a rickshaw puller from Nanjing, saw that Shi was a gullible country bumpkin. Because the crabs he was carrying were slightly larger than usual, he gathered several companions, stopped Shi, cut open the bamboo basket with a knife, reached in and took five or six large crabs, and turned to leave. Shi was angry that they had taken his crabs without asking, and stepped forward to scold them. Chen glared at him and said, "What's the big deal about me taking four or five of your crabs? You should know that you have to pay taxes for carrying crabs here. If you know what's good for you, give me forty cents, or else you can forget about going home to eat crabs." Then, Chen snatched the crab basket and had his companions take it away. Shi was anxious and immediately grabbed Chen and reported to Qian Dianjia, the guard at Post No. 15, who brought him to the First Precinct of the First District. He was ordered to stay temporarily, pending preliminary review and handling by the chief of the precinct.

Letters to the Editor 241

To the Editor,

I recently read in the October 24th edition of your paper that in the case of Tang Yueqing enticing Luo Yuying, Luo Yuying had first gone to the Zhongfa Watch Shop upstairs on West Xinqiao Street in the French Concession to meet with a friend of Tang's. We have checked and the entire building above our shop is not subleased to others, and none of our employees know anyone named Tang Yueqing. As this concerns the reputation of our shop, we hope you will correct this matter.

Zhongfa Watch Shop, October 24th

To the Editor,

The content of the news regarding the death of Yang Heshang and Mo Bu, published in your newspaper on October 23rd, involves me and is not in accordance with the facts. I am writing to request a correction to avoid confusion. My adopted son, Zhifu, was two months old when he was sent to my care by his biological father, Yang Heshang, and is now nineteen years old. In these nineteen years, I have paid for his upbringing, education, and engagement, at great expense. The Yang family has not paid a single cent. Since this year, the Yang family has intended to take Zhifu back to their family to continue their lineage. On September 14th, Yang Heshang and his wife, along with his brother Ruihua and his mother-in-law, Fan, invited me to discuss taking him back. The Yang family voluntarily offered 500 yuan as compensation for the expenses of raising, educating, and engaging him. The adopted son, Zhifu, was taken back by Yang Heshang and his wife, his brother, and Fan, that same evening at 7:00 PM. As for the compensation, not a single cent has been paid to date. I have never coerced or demanded payment. I am writing to briefly state the above, and I request that it be published in the Letters to the Editor column to make a correction. I rely on your public spirit.

Sincerely, Kang Jinbao, October 24th, to the editor of Shen Bao.

To the Editor,

Hu Changsheng and Chen Fucai, staff members of the May 30th Family Association, and Xu Zhijian, a small businessman, and Luo Wenlang, a relative of a victim, had filed lawsuits against each other in the Special District Court for embezzlement, slander, and other charges. After several court hearings, it was discovered that the embezzler was someone else, and had no relationship to the parties involved in the mutual accusations. The three parties separately requested that the case be dismissed in court. Luo Wenlang's losses were compensated by Hu Changsheng, Xu Zhijian, and others from the Family Association. During the previous lawsuit, your newspaper and other newspapers published various details, which affected the reputation of Hu and Chen of the Family Association. Now that a settlement has been reached, Luo Wenlang and Xu Zhijian both feel apologetic towards Hu and Chen. I, the undersigned lawyer, am writing on behalf of Xu Zhijian to declare the previous situation to your newspaper, and I respectfully request that it be published in the Letters to the Editor column, in order to reveal the truth.

Sincerely, lawyer Li Shirui, October 24, year 19, to the reporters of the Shen Bao.

Page 23

Social News

Southward Journey 244

— Moye

Jinan Correspondence

Westerners enjoy traveling for leisure, while Chinese people consider going out as a last resort. Getting on and off boats and cars is like desperately escaping for one's life, and being confined to a corner is no different from a prison life. The reporter, on a southward journey, took the Tianjin-Pukou train. The distance was only a thousand li, but it took a whole day and night. After being exhausted, my muscles and bones ached. Even after resting for a night, I still had not recovered. I heard that a passenger between Jinan and Pukou fell off the top of a train while crossing a steel bridge, resulting in shattered bones. I couldn't help but feel horrified. Fortunately, I haven't reached the point of having to climb on the top of the train. It has been ten days since the Jinan-Pukou line reopened, but second-class tickets have only been sold for two days. It is said that this is the result of Director Wang Duanting of the Tianjin Bureau's negotiations in Jinan. However, although there are second-class cars, there are actually only five private rooms. Deputy Director Zhu Lvyun of the Tianjin Bureau has already occupied one of them, and the rest are reserved for foreigners from the Yuzhong Lishunde Hotel and Chinese VIPs. The reporter wanted to buy a second-class ticket on a temporary basis, but was given a blank stare by the ticket seller, who said that he had to book a private room a day in advance and did not sell temporary single tickets. The reporter was angry and wanted to buy a third-class ticket, but in fact, the number of tickets had already exceeded the capacity of the car. Even if he wanted to buy a ticket, he would have to queue up behind more than a hundred hypocrites. Calculating that there were only half an hour left before the departure time, I was afraid that I would be rejected. So, I swallowed my anger and negotiated with the stationmaster. Fortunately, I was helped to find a seat outside the second-class car's bedroom, bought a second-class ticket, and squatted outside the bedroom door. I dared not lie down for long, nor could I sit upright. I bent over and crossed my legs, like a snail. It was truly an adventure.

The departure was originally scheduled for 7:30 AM, but the engine moved back and forth, and it was almost 8:00 AM. The villagers who had already bought tickets were all scrambling to the top. The long line of people behind, seeing that the ticket booth's small window was closed, were still unwilling to disperse, probably waiting to line up like this until the next morning. When the train passed Liangwangzhuang, driven by curiosity, the reporter climbed out of the crowd and went to visit the third-class car. Looking inside from outside the window, I could only see heads shaking. I couldn't tell how many there were. Many children were crying because they were squeezed, and it was difficult for women to even turn around while breastfeeding. The people sitting on top of the car were proudly congratulating themselves for catching the train, forgetting the bitter cold winds and rain in the evening.

The train stopped for a long time after passing Cangzhou. I took a stroll on the platform to get some fresh air. I saw the slogan "Spiritual Revolution" still visible on the wall of the station. I remembered that last year, when Jiang went north, the Jin army generals Fu Zuoyi, Li Shengda, and the former mayor Cui Tingxian accompanied He Chengjun on a special train to wait here. It has only been a year, and they have become public figures due to the rebellion. The prestige of famous generals has also disappeared like the turbid waters of the Fei River. I couldn't help but sigh at the vicissitudes of the world.

Ticket Prices for the Qitian Stage on October 25th 245
