Page 24

The train arrived in Dezhou, where ten thousand homes were lit up, and a strange scene of changing trains between the North and South was also being performed at this moment. It is necessary to record its inside story. Since the Jin army withdrew, the Jinpu Railway Bureau has been planning to restore traffic. The Southern Bureau first sent Deputy Director Zhu Lüyun to Tianjin to discuss the reception method. After understanding from all parties, the seal was received on the 3rd, and it was planned to restore the office. However, the next day, Qu Yucheng, the deputy director of the Tianjin Bureau, suddenly received an order from the Northeast authorities to be appointed as the director. As a result, the Southern Bureau's planned traffic plan was suspended. However, traffic is not only a necessity for the people, but also related to the income of the Railway Bureau itself. Therefore, the Northern Bureau sent Wang Duanting, the head of the vehicle affairs department, to Jinan to discuss the exchange of locomotives. Seeing the trains running in opposite directions, the income was settled separately by region. The detailed content is unknown. The general conditions are as follows: The No. 9 passenger and freight train from Tainan opened to Dezhou, and the original locomotive No. 107 returned to Tianjin as the No. 10 train locomotive. The No. 10 train locomotive then towed the No. 9 train back to Jinan. If the No. 9 train did not see the No. 10 train coming, it would stop in Dezhou and proceed after it had passed. The same was true if the No. 10 train arrived first. If the number of vehicles coming from the other side was less than the number of vehicles leaving, several vehicles to be leaving would be detached, ensuring that the number on both sides was equal. The Northern Bureau did not have second-class cars. For the convenience of passengers and public officials, the Southern Bureau lent one car. The income from tickets and freight was calculated and accounted for by both parties with Sangyuan on the border of Hebei Province as the boundary. The above are the main conditions for the Tianjin-Jinan line to be able to reach directly. When the reporter accompanied the train through Dezhou, he personally saw both parties clearly explain before they drove off in opposite directions. The only hardship was that the time when the trains from both sides met in Dezhou varied greatly, so the reporter's train stopped in Dezhou for as long as two hours. What was even more difficult was that the incoming train was short of three ticket cars. The stationmaster calculated that the numbers were incorrect, so he ordered the train the reporter was riding to detach three vehicles. As a result, the general public who were ignorant of the world and the ants in the car were in trouble. After those in the car got off, they could no longer enjoy the blessing of being crowded. They had to compete to "get on top". Those who were originally on top still got on top after getting off. Between getting on and off, moving luggage was frequent, and it was inconvenient to chase them away in the dark. So, with a sound, the train started. However, there were still many people left on the station. The station staff was still scolding, "Damn it, hurry up!" The train drove far away, and the sound of "leave, leave" could still be heard. The feeling of unhappiness was as painful as being stabbed in the heart with a knife. I had to curl up in the daze, hearing the sound of water dripping from the roof of the car. The waiter scolded loudly, but there was no way to stop it. According to the workers of the Railway Bureau, the Jinpu Railway Bureau has been unlucky since the Lincheng robbery. The directors in the middle have been changed several times, and Han Wenyu and Sun Ziven are the most guilty. Han created the precedent of deducting wages and owing salaries, and Sun used the evil habit of buying vacancies with money and falsely filling them. However, at that time, there were still five trains a day, two express trains directly to Pukou, and three distance trains. If calculated in opposite directions, there were ten trains on the way every day, not including the fifty blue steel cars. Now, the steel cars are stored in the Northeast and Shi Yousan's place, and the remaining trains are not enough for three. With these three trains, the whole line reaches directly, and it is still worried that it is not enough, let alone divided into two bureaus in the North and South, each acting on its own. The easiest business in the world to make money is the train, but in China, it has been losing money year after year, and foreign debts are difficult to repay. Although his words were painful, they were also true. This train should have arrived in Jinan at 8:00 pm that night, but as a result of "stopping at every station and stopping for a long time", it arrived at 4:00 am the next morning. In the daze, I was kicked awake by the waiter who was carrying luggage, and I felt sore all over. At the same time, I felt that my legs were no longer mine. I reluctantly stumbled off the train, as if in a dream. I heard someone from Kaifeng say that the Longhai Line from Xuzhou to Shanghai takes two nights and one day to reach, and stops at each station for one hour. The wheels of the train run like a mule cart. After listening to the words, I felt as if my brain had been poked with a small awl. (17th)

Social News Submission Guidelines 293

(1) The text should be limited to news about domestic and foreign science, industry, commerce, rural areas

(2) Hygiene, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life. The picture should be limited to various lyrical paintings about social life.

(3) Photos that are qualified are those related to seasons, scenery, animals, people, and news photography. Photos of beautiful women in seasonal and scenic photography are especially welcome.

(4) The number of words in each article should not exceed 2,000.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(6) Do not write the manuscript horizontally, the words should not be scrawled, and Western writing can be omitted. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the interpretation.

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw the picture, and do not use colored paper, you must use white paper and black drawing.

(8) Please indicate that the submission is for the Social News Editorial Department.

(9) Whether the submitted manuscript is published or not, it will not be returned. If you need to return it, you should declare it in advance.
